Dissatisfaction with Japan's Position on Abyssinia: Anti-Japanese Sentiment is High in Italy; Believed to be Disrupting European Peace and Unity; Simultaneously Reproaches Britain for Lifting the Arms Embargo 29

(Rome) Anti-Japanese sentiment is becoming increasingly intense today, almost shifting public attention away from the government's abolition of the 40% gold reserve for banknotes. Prime Minister Mussolini's official newspaper severely criticized Japan for inciting Abyssinia to resist Italy and violating the Kellogg-Briand Pact, and hoping to undermine the unity of Britain, France, and Italy in maintaining European peace. The newspaper further stated that Japan is caught in the dream of imperialism, obviously seeking to take the place of white people in Africa. Today, four armed policemen and two plainclothes detectives patrol in front of the Japanese Embassy for protection. (July 23rd, National Telegram)

(Rome) Italians are indignant because Japan is favoring Abyssinia. Today, a special guard is stationed in front of the Japanese Embassy to prevent accidents. At the same time, Italian newspapers are also conducting anti-Japanese propaganda. The Italian People's Newspaper stated that Japan's new attitude contradicts the statement made by Sugimura, the Japanese Ambassador to Italy, that Japan has no political relationship with Abyssinia. Japan's sudden expression of sympathy for the poor and barren Abyssinia proves its ambition to carry out unlimited political and economic development in Africa as a new base for attacking Europe. A report that anti-Japanese demonstrations took place in Milan and three other places yesterday has been denied by semi-official sources, saying that the excitement of the people in the three cities was caused by Mussolini's recent declaration on Abyssinia. The anti-Japanese movement has not diminished the Italian attacks on Britain in recent weeks. The famous political writer, Gaida, wrote an article in the newspapers, saying that the British cabinet's decision not to prohibit the export of arms to both Italy and Abyssinia is clear evidence of Anglo-Abyssinian unity. (July 24th, Reuters Telegram)

(Tokyo) The Asahi Shimbun today published an article that appears to be authorized by the authorities, saying that the Ministry of Foreign Affairs is very indignant about the anti-Japanese propaganda in the Italian newspapers. The Italian newspapers are deliberately fostering a hostile public opinion towards Japan and engaging in an orderly conspiracy to develop the Italo-Abyssinian dispute into a war between colored people and white people. The Italians hope to use this method to force Britain and France to protect Italy's policies. Japan is now on guard, not wanting to be manipulated by the Italians. Japan is now watching the development of the Italo-Abyssinian dispute with a calm and cautious attitude. The spokesman of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs met with the press this morning to discuss the Italian newspapers' attitude towards Japan. A reporter asked whether Japanese newspapers would remain silent if Italian newspapers provoked Japan in this way. The spokesman replied that the opinions of Japanese newspapers are different from the news published in countries with freedom of speech. The spokesman finally said that the Japanese government is considering sending an ambassador to Abyssinia in January next year. (July 24th, Reuters Telegram)

Abyssinian Emperor's 42nd Birthday Celebrated in the Palace; Italian Envoy Absent; Japanese Emperor Sends Telegram of Congratulations 30

(London) The situation of the Abyssinian Emperor's birthday yesterday was reported by the Times correspondent in the Abyssinian capital as follows: Before dawn, the residents were awakened from their sleep by a 21-gun salute. In the early morning, the streets were crowded with people. Numerous infantrymen surrounded the soldiers of various tribes and many chieftains who came from all over to pay their respects, winding into the city. Each chieftain was riding on a donkey and holding a velvet flag as a symbol of paying respects. Flags were hung all over the city. Then, at 9:00 a.m., the emperor, dressed in ordinary clothes, ascended the palace, surrounded by cabinet ministers and advisors. On the palace steps in front of the palace, there were modern guards standing on both sides. There were also officers with decorated lion manes, holding spears and shields, and wearing gorgeous crowns, ascending the palace. Then the officers of the guards and representatives of the diplomatic corps paid their respects to the emperor. After the ceremony, five thousand soldiers held a grand meat feast, and the emperor also participated in it. On this day, only the governor of Waleka Province, who was far away in the extreme west and not affected by the situation, was able to leave his post to come to the capital to celebrate the birthday. The other governors were all at their posts and could not come to the capital. Moreover, of the diplomatic corps, only the Italian envoy to Abyssinia, Grigulucci, was absent. The Abyssinian side believed that the celebration ceremony was grand, more attentive than the palaces of European countries. The Italian envoy's absence was a serious insult, but the Abyssinian government decided not to pursue it. (July 24th, Havas Telegram)

(Abyssinian Capital) Today is the 42nd birthday of the King of Abyssinia. After a 21-gun salute, the King sat on the throne in the old palace to receive the congratulations of the princes, ministers, and envoys of various countries. The Belgian envoy, Johnson, delivered the congratulations of the envoys on behalf of the diplomatic corps. The Italian envoy and consulate staff did not participate. The Japanese Emperor also sent a telegram of congratulations, which is considered very important by political circles here and will arouse anti-Japanese propaganda in the Italian newspapers. When the American representative entered the city after the ceremony, an incident occurred. The crowd surrounded his car, waving flags and shouting "Long live America!" This enthusiastic expression was due to the US government's permission for officers to join the Abyssinian army and the American Red Cross's willingness to provide assistance. The British fear a large-scale air raid on the Abyssinian capital, and the embassy authorities have made proper defense arrangements to avoid being bombed. (July 23rd, National Telegram)

Japanese Urge Italy to Draw Back from the Brink; Also Aware of "International Justice" 31

Therefore, Abyssinia's arrogance today is largely due to Britain's assistance. Finally, the newspaper warned the British government that Britain's lifting of the arms export ban has created a major bad precedent in the international community. (July 24th, National Telegram)

Japanese Swords Dedicated to the Abyssinian Emperor 33

Ogura: The Japan Sword Craftsmen's Association dedicated a Japanese sword to the Emperor of Abyssinia, who is about to go to war with Italy, in the spirit of Japanese-Abyssinian friendship. Mr. Koshizu Iwaoka, a director of the Association, recently sought information from sword craftsmen in various parts of Kyushu. As a result of the research, it was decided to dedicate a sword forged by Mitsunori Kaneko of Tagawa County, Fukuoka Prefecture. Member of Parliament Hikosaburo Kurihara requested Foreign Minister Hirota to mediate the matter. (July 24th, Dentsu Telegram)

Italo-Abyssinian Dispute: League of Nations to Discuss Comprehensively; British Proposal Supported by France 34

(London) Reuters diplomatic correspondent has learned that when the League of Nations Executive Council meets next week to consider the Italo-Abyssinian dispute, the British government intends to urge a comprehensive discussion. The hope of resolving the dispute peacefully before the Executive Council meets is now very slim. After French Prime Minister and Foreign Minister Laval held talks with British Ambassador to Paris, Clark, it is expected that the British proposal for a comprehensive discussion will be supported by France. Britain recently sought a basis for discussion in Rome and learned that the Italian government will not be satisfied unless it annexes Abyssinia or at least obtains political control of part or all of Abyssinia. At that time, the possibility of convening a meeting of the three countries that signed the 1906 treaty (Britain, France, and Italy) was also discussed, but unless Italy guarantees not to resort to force, the meeting will be difficult to convene. British Ambassador to Rome, Sir Drummond, urged Italy to thoroughly state its case against Abyssinia in Geneva, but Italy still does not seem to want to do this. If Italy insists on this attitude, the situation will become tense when the League of Nations Executive Council meets in the future and invokes Article 12 of the League of Nations Covenant. It is expected that the British representative attending the Executive Council meeting will be Eden, Minister without Portfolio. (Note: Article 12 of the League of Nations Covenant states that if a dispute arises between members of the League of Nations that is likely to lead to a rupture, the matter should be submitted to arbitration or to the Executive Council for review, and it is agreed that in any case, war shall not be waged until three months after the arbitrators' judgment or the Executive Council's report has expired.) (July 24th, Reuters Telegram)

(London) According to observations by diplomatic circles, it is difficult to resolve the Italo-Abyssinian dispute through diplomatic channels before the League of Nations Executive Council meets, because Italy will not agree to promise not to engage in war during the negotiations. France has now accepted that the League of Nations will conduct a comprehensive study of the Italo-Abyssinian dispute. Diplomatic circles are very satisfied with this. However, the rumor that Britain and France have reached an agreement on the procedures for resolving the dispute in accordance with Article 15 of the League of Nations Covenant has not been confirmed. (According to Section 7 of Article 15, if the members of the Executive Council, except for the representative(s) of one or more of the disputing parties, cannot unanimously approve the report, the member states of the League of Nations reserve the right to take the necessary actions they deem necessary to maintain fairness and justice.) In general, political circles mostly agree to invoke Article 12 of the Covenant to deal with the Italo-Abyssinian dispute. (July 23rd, Havas Telegram)

(Paris) The date of the League of Nations Executive Council meeting must be decided today when League of Nations Secretary-General Avenol consults with Prime Minister Laval. Newspapers this morning stated that it can now be determined that the League of Nations Executive Council will meet at the end of this month. The only thing that has not been decided is how long the meeting will last, but the main issues will not be discussed until the end of August. According to the "Warfare" newspaper, officials believe that Italy will definitely attend the meeting, but the Italians require the powers to guarantee that the debate will not deviate from a certain scope. Therefore, the entire issue is expected to come to a temporary conclusion within 48 hours. Compulsory resolutions and the invocation of Article 15 of the League of Nations Covenant will have to wait until the League of Nations meeting at the end of August to be discussed. (July 24th, National Telegram)

(Paris) Semi-official sources confirmed that the British and French governments have agreed to convene the League of Nations Executive Council for discussion within the next week. The date will be determined by Soviet Foreign Minister Litvinov, Chairman of the Executive Council. Mr. Litvinov is expected to arrive in Paris by Thursday. It is now understood that the Italo-Abyssinian issue will be discussed in accordance with Article 15 of the League of Nations Covenant. (July 23rd, National Telegram)

Abyssinian Envoy Expresses Unwillingness to Cede an Inch of Land; Italy's Ambition to Annex Abyssinia: A Trigger for a World War 35

(Paris) The Abyssinian envoy to Britain, Martin, recently gave an interview to a reporter from the "Paris Echo," expressing pessimism about the Italo-Abyssinian dispute. He said, "A compromise solution is not easy to achieve. The Italian side has already spent more than ten million lire on military expenses, and its army sent to Africa has more than 200,000 men. How can we expect them to stop the war plan? Moreover, what Italy seeks is not just economic concessions, but the annexation of our country. Even if we give economic concessions or even territorial concessions to Italy, we cannot know what the result will be. The country's desires are increasing day by day. Looking at the past, I am deeply moved. Emperor Menelik once gave a large piece of land, Eritrea, to Italy, but Italy's desires were not satisfied. This can be seen." Martin continued, "Abyssinia should protect its independence with an indomitable spirit. The Italo-Abyssinian dispute is still very serious for Britain. Once Italy invades Abyssinia, Egypt and British Sudan will be threatened, and the balance of power along the Red Sea will also be shaken, benefiting Italy and harming Britain. In other words, the route from Europe to India will be threatened by Italy. In short, once the Italo-Abyssinian war breaks out, its scope will extend beyond local warfare and become a trigger for conflict between colored people and white colonial countries." Martin also said, "If Britain and France are willing to cede a portion of their colonies to Italy as compensation, they can do so themselves. Abyssinia will never cede an inch of land." (July 24th, Havas Telegram)

Italian Currency Devaluation: Gold Bloc Anxious 36

Italy Explains the Purpose of Abolishing Gold Reserves: Hoping to Avoid Misunderstandings Abroad

(Tokyo) Regarding Italy's suspension of the legal reserve clause of the central bank, Japanese foreign exchange banks observe as follows: Italy's distress lies in the stagnation of foreign trade. Other purely economic reasons, such as the decline in foreign tourist spending and remittances from immigrants, are the main reasons for the devaluation. This suspension is only using the Italo-Abyssinian dispute as an excuse to avoid criticism from the gold bloc countries and to carry out the devaluation to increase its competitiveness in the international economy. If the devaluation of the Italian currency is realized, the Laval cabinet in France seems to have escaped the crisis, and the anxiety of the European gold bloc countries will become more intense. (July 24th, Dentsu News Agency Telegram)

(Rome) In order to avoid misunderstandings caused by the abolition of the 40% gold reserve for Italian currency, the official statement issued today stated that the plan adopted yesterday concerning gold reserves had no effect on the currency value. The Italian government will restore the 40% gold reserve in the near future. The plan adopted yesterday was because the debt owed to foreigners reached 500,000,000 lire, which urgently needed to be repaid. Therefore, the government had no choice but to amend the gold reserve law. The government has now been able to repay all debts, and the debt owed to foreign countries was used by the government to purchase raw materials. (July 23rd, National News Agency Telegram)

Netherlands to Maintain Current Monetary Policy 37

The Hague: Today, the Dutch cabinet issued a statement expressing the Collin government's determination to maintain the gold standard. The statement said that as long as the government exists, it will continue to do its best to reject the policy of currency devaluation. At the same time, to avoid the tide of cabinet changes, it has asked the Lower House to adjourn. The Lower House, with the support of the Catholic Party for the government's economic bill, also wants to give the government a chance to reconsider. However, according to a statement issued by the Catholic Party, although the party members are prepared to support the Collin cabinet's economic laws, they are still unwilling to give it a vote of confidence. Prime Minister Collin claimed that he was prepared to ask Queen Wilhelmina of the Netherlands to consider the policy to deal with the situation. According to political circles, Collin and the cabinet may submit their resignations, but the Queen may dissolve Parliament and retain Collin. (July 24th, National Telegram)

Content of Japan's Reply to Egypt's Notification of Treaty Abolition 41

Friendly Relations Between the Two Countries Have Always Been Good; Hoping to Negotiate and Conclude a New Commercial Treaty

(Tokyo) The Egyptian government submitted a memorandum on the 18th notifying the abolition of the Japanese-Egyptian Treaty of Commerce. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs decided to have Consul General Amaki personally deliver a reply in the near future. The content seems to be to urge the Egyptian government to reflect. The general situation is recorded as follows: (1) In its memorandum, the Egyptian government stated that Japanese-Egyptian trade is one-sided in that imports exceed exports, and pointed out the actual situation. However, the figures it cited differ greatly from the Japanese statistical figures. Moreover, the total amount of Japanese imports from Egypt has recently increased significantly. The total number of Egyptian imports in the first half of this year reached 32 million yuan, while Japanese exports to Egypt were only 25 million yuan. Japan is in a situation where imports exceed exports. (2) The Egyptian government has always advocated the conclusion of a new treaty to replace the Japanese-Egyptian Treaty of Commerce, and based on the protection of Egyptian domestic industries. If Japanese exports to Egypt threaten the country's domestic industries, the precedent of the Indo-Japanese negotiations should be followed and measures should be discussed to resolve the issue. However, the Egyptian government did not do this and suddenly announced the abolition of the Treaty of Commerce. The procedure is somewhat regrettable. (3) Japan has always been friendly to Egypt, and will continue its friendly relations in the future. Therefore, the budget for this year also includes the funds needed to establish a Japanese branch embassy in Cairo, and preparations are underway. As for trade relations, Japan will do its best to respect Egypt's intentions and attempt to adjust its relations. Therefore, the Egyptian government should also be based on facts as much as possible when handling the aftermath of the abolition of the old treaty and concluding a new treaty, and try to deal with it properly. It is hoped that this will be the case. (July 24th, Japan Associated Press Telegram)

After the Expiration of the London Treaty, Britain Will Begin Building Warships 43

Existing Ships Are Mostly Decayed and Unsuitable

(London) The Daily Telegraph today published an article by Bywater, stating that after the expiration of the London Naval Treaty in December 1936, Britain will immediately begin building sixty cruisers. Currently, the number of British warships is limited to fifty. The naval review held at Spithead to commemorate the King's Jubilee included a total of one hundred and fifty-seven warships of various sizes. While the appearance was formidable, many members of Parliament felt that the majority of the warships were no longer effective, and the combat equipment lacked efficiency, leaving them with an unpleasant impression. Few ships were of the new type, while a large number were decayed and unsuitable for combat. This has sparked comments from all sides. Of the eleven battleships that the British Navy currently prides itself on, only the HMS Royal Oak and HMS Hood are of the latest type, but they were launched more than ten years ago. The Queen Elizabeth-class battleships are over twenty years old, and their speed is nominally twenty-five knots, but this has been greatly reduced after being fitted with heavy armor. By the time the London Naval Treaty expires, half of Britain's cruisers, half of its destroyers, and one-third of its submarines will be nearing the end of their service life. This is the main argument of those who oppose the Anglo-German naval agreement. Critics argue that all German warships in the future will be of the new type. The article concludes by saying that Admiral Sir Roger Keyes and former First Lord of the Admiralty Winston Churchill have requested raising a naval loan to repair the ships that are unsuitable for modern warfare, and support for this is growing. (Reuters, 24th)

The United States Hopes for the Reopening of the Naval Conference, Still Insisting on Maintaining Superiority over Japan, and the Bill to Increase Naval Officers Has Been Signed by Roosevelt 44

(Washington) According to official sources today, the United States still hopes that Britain will convene the 1935 naval conference. Experts here also claim that Britain's abandonment of the ratio system is aimed at gaining Japan's approval for other alternative plans, making the British Navy the standard for other countries. The word "ratio" creates the perception of inequality for countries whose navies are below the maximum limit. Therefore, future efforts in international disarmament will be based on the principles of equality or security. It is worth noting that the United States, with its longer coastline, should have more warships if it actually wants to be on an equal footing with Japan. (National Telegraph, 23rd)

A Record of Inspecting the Disaster Situation of the Rivers 95

— By Geng Ya, Special Correspondent of This Newspaper

From Shanghai to Hankou (Continued)

On the border of Anhui and Jiangxi, opposite Madang, the Mahua Dam, which belongs to Pengze in Jiangxi and Qiu Pu Dongliu, collapsed in two or three places successively in the early part of this month due to the difficulty of discharging accumulated water internally and the fierce impact of the flood externally. Villages and fields in the levee within the two provinces were all submerged, and the losses were incalculable. According to reports, the dam is fifteen feet wide and rises a few inches to a few feet above the water level. Its collapse was not due to overflowing and washing away, but to a sudden collapse. The new dam had not yet been built firmly, resulting in seepage of trickle, which led to a major disaster. Going west from Anqing, the disaster situation becomes more severe. Where the dikes are intact, the seedlings are green and a good harvest can still be expected. If the dikes collapse, there is a vast expanse of water with no trace of crops. Only an occasional willow tree can be seen, which can be used to measure the shape of the fields. In several places, the river surface and the levee are much higher than the fields on both sides, and the tails of the houses are also below the water level. Once the river dike collapses, the torrent rages and becomes uncontrollable. The disaster area is extremely large, and the floodwater is difficult to recede in a short time due to the excessive height of the levee, making the disaster even worse than the Yellow River disaster. Therefore, the way to control the river is not only to increase the height of the dikes, but also to pay close attention to the dredging of the waterways.

The water in Jiujiang is also on the shore, and each road such as No. 1, 2, 3, Da Zhong, and Binjiang are three or four feet deep. Pedestrians mostly use rickshaws or small boats as transportation. Residents beside Gan Tang Lake live in water. A section of Lushan Road is also flooded and cannot be driven on. Most of the internal lakes have overflowed. More than a hundred civil levees in the Poyang Lake area have collapsed. According to reports, the water disaster area in Jiangxi Province this time is as many as forty-five counties. The disasters were all caused by continuous rain and floods. For example, the water level in various villages in Wuyuan and the West Gate are all higher than the city walls. The refugees in Guixi are floating on the roofs, crying for help with no response, and countless deaths. All thirty-eight levees in Yongxiu were washed away, drowning more than a thousand people. In the newly built flood, starvation and hunger are intertwined, and there are more cases of people who eat grass to relieve their hunger and die from abdominal distension. The tragic situation is unbearable to hear.

Passing through Wuxue at noon on the 19th, the lower part of the riverside houses was submerged in water. The ship did not dock and only took a distant photo. Xu Shiying, Chairman of the China Relief Council, and his party of six came west to survey the disaster. Although we were fortunate to be on the same ship, Mr. Xu looked far away with a telescope while the ship was traveling, and referred to the maps. When the ship stopped, he inspected and guided the local defenses. He was worried and worked hard all day long, and rarely had the opportunity to talk to the outside world. On the evening when he was about to arrive in Hankou, I made a special request to ask him about his feelings.

The main points of the conversation are roughly as follows: "The ability of local officials and people to defend against disasters this time is better than before, but the social economy and the ability to provide disaster relief are far worse than before. We are discussing with the authorities of various provinces the urgent measures to revitalize industry and address both the symptoms and root causes. The central government will do its best to provide subsidies. After receiving the actual situation in various places in the future, we will truthfully report to the central government to make it clear about the severity of the flood disaster and the suffering of the people. As for the way to control the water, unless huge funds are raised (approximately 500 million yuan in total) and a comprehensive plan is made, and the Jianghuai and Han rivers are fundamentally treated, the water damage in the future will be even worse than this time." According to another piece of information, Mr. Xu already has a relatively feasible good plan for raising huge funds for water control, but it has not yet been approved by the central government, so the announcement is still pending.

Arrived in Hankou the next morning, unloaded luggage at the hotel, and went to the nearby Jiang Han Guan area. The water level was 50.7 feet, which was slightly lower than before, but the Linjiang Road outside the embankment was still being impacted by the river water. From time to time, a turtle was rolled up by the waves and dried on the embankment slope. A child caught it and wanted to take it home, but everyone was afraid of offending the Dragon King and insisted on releasing it back into the river. Although this is a superstitious detail, it also shows the inner fear of the crowd. The ditch water that leaked out of the various roads into the river was specially equipped with a drainage machine to pour it over the levee into the river because the river water was higher than the road surface, fearing the impact of backflow. In the few days before the water level was higher, the citizens were terrified of the pain of the twenty years ago, and most of them moved their homes from low to high places. The important stocks of shops also moved to the second and third floors.

Crossing the river to the Xujiapeng station on the Yuehan Railway, I saw that the railway of a certain transshipment company had been washed away for tens of feet. The station pier was even connected with unroofed iron cars as a bridge. Although walking was very stable, it was a pity that it was an underutilization of materials. Many of the nearby houses were also drifting in the water. Looking at the watermarks on their doors and windows, some were duck-yellow with a hint of green, about a foot above the water surface, which was the water level that had made people horrified a few days ago. A foot higher, there was still a light brown color, which was the tragic trace of the great flood twenty years ago. When the reporter was taking pictures in the mirror, I saw a pale-faced young woman on the flooded building, leaning on the railing and holding a child, shaking and humming, "Maomao, don't cry anymore. Someone is here to inspect the flood. We will have something to eat soon. Maomao, don't cry..." Hearing this, I felt unspeakable pain in my heart. However, the most tragic places in Wuhan are probably still in Zhanggongdi, Danshuichi, Shaijiashan, Jinyintan, and Gushushu. This is just a small part of it.

Hubei Province is surrounded by the Jianghan rivers, and is known as a land of lakes. Every summer and autumn, it suffers from floods and disasters. The scars of the twentieth and twenty-second years have not yet healed, and this autumn it has suffered its misfortune again. In the upper reaches, the floods shook the valleys, and the mountains collapsed. In the lower reaches, the floods rushed and raged, with thousands of miles of water. As of the 22nd, the number of counties that have reported disaster situations to the provincial government has reached as many as forty-nine. According to what Mr. Xu Zhen, the committee chairman, and his party obtained by looking down from the air, all the ten or so counties in the upper reaches of Jianghan were vast expanses of water. In the central region, such as Tianmen and Hanchuan, the disaster situation was the most serious, and the entire territory was in the water. Others who could see the tops of city walls, roofs, and treetops were also very few in number. Hundreds of thousands of disaster victims have been displaced and are all waiting to be rescued.

The scene of people walking on the boardwalk on Jiujiang Road that was flooded

The houses of Xujiapeng in Wuchang were flooded

Wang Yongbin Talks About the Purpose of His Inspection Tour of Seven Provinces:督促廓淸宿案指導推行新法 96

Supervise the Clearing of Old Cases and Guide the Implementation of New Laws

Wang Yongbin, Minister of Justice and Administration, had a plan to inspect the actual judicial situation in various provinces at the beginning of his tenure. Later, due to the complexity of departmental affairs, the date of departure was repeatedly delayed. Because the new criminal law and the three-level three-trial system were promulgated and implemented, it would be a month, Wang used his department's important official duties, dealing with them late into the night, hoping to set off at the end of this month. His inspection route is scheduled to be Shandong, Hebei, Chahar, Suiyuan, Shanxi, Shaanxi, and Henan provinces. He plans to spend a month to be able to return to Beijing to attend the National Judicial Conference, which will open in mid-September. The Daily News reporter asked about the main objectives of this inspection tour as Wang's departure approached yesterday. He was informed one by one, and his talks are recorded as follows.

Guide the Implementation of New Laws

Wang said first that after the implementation of the new criminal law, the new criminal procedure law, the civil procedure law, and the three-level three-trial system, the ministry had already sent special commissioners to various places to supervise and guide. However, it is necessary to personally inspect the progress of the implementation in various provinces and whether the accumulated cases have been cleared. The intention of the central government to change the legal system is to reduce the accidental spiritual and material damage to the parties. The first step in the current implementation is to clear the accumulated cases, so that both trial and execution can benefit. During this trip, I will strictly set deadlines to urge the clearing of old cases, and at the same time provide detailed guidance to ensure that the implementation of the new law is without any ambiguity. When the national legal system is just beginning to change, the implementing agencies will inevitably encounter difficulties and doubts, and need to be instructed and explained.

Correct the Style of Prolonging Detention

In the past, local judicial organs often conducted detailed investigations and collected evidence for criminal cases, prolonging the judgment, and involving various criminals. Many of them have been detained in the detention center for many years without being interrogated. For example, recently in a certain place, an old man in his eighties was arrested for a minor case. As a result, he died in the detention center because he could not bear the suffering of being imprisoned. This kind of thing is really uneasy on the conscience. If the case is settled early, the crimes that the criminals should be punished for can be executed quickly, and those who are suspected of being wronged can also be cleared and rehabilitated early. If the case is delayed, not only will the innocent suffer the pain of detention for nothing, but the criminals will also increase the suffering of detention, and even the detention period will exceed the sentence. It is contrary to the spirit of national rule of law and the loss of national production and people's lives and careers. This trend, if not strictly corrected, will not only fail to empty the prisons, but will also lead to overcrowding. Therefore, I must try to correct it on this trip.

Dredge Inmate in Custody

I will pay special attention to the dredging of detainees in detention centers in various places. Prisons are places where convicted criminals serve their sentences, and only need to investigate their food, hygiene, education, and facilities. Detention centers are places of custody. Those who are detained have not been determined whether they have committed a crime. It is also common for good citizens to be detained because of slight suspicion. The treatment, equipment, and handling should be slightly better than prisons. But in fact, detention centers in various places are simplified, and the number of detainees is increasing year by year, due to the increase in criminal cases in recent years. The dredging of detention centers is a more pressing issue. The Legislative Yuan has passed a method of dredging prisoners, and the dredging of detention centers is only to urge bail and speedy settlement of cases.

Tell the Conscience Responsibility

Wang said at the end that on this tour, I will tell all judicial officials to emphasize that "the moral character of judges should be equally important as their conscientious responsibility" He could not consider the actual pain and damage suffered by the parties involved. This is because their duties as judges are flawless, but their conscientious responsibility is lacking. For example, in the past, local judges often detained those who could be detained or not detained, and prosecuted those who could be prosecuted or not prosecuted. When their judgments were executed, they were often reluctant to grant probation and parole, seeking only to reduce their own responsibilities, and disregarding the pain of those who suffered. If this is the case, how can it be in line with the spirit of the national legislation to set up this lenient provision? It is reported that the provinces that Wang plans to inspect on this trip are all areas that the former Minister Luo Wengan did not go to. Yang Peng, Counselor of the Ministry, Wang Dengdi, Section Chief, Liao Weixun, Secretary Chen Daqi and other five people will accompany the inspection. It is reported that Wang will also inspect some courts in Jiangsu and Anhui provinces on his way back when time permits. (Daily News)

Songjiang 97

Section Chief Inspects Seawall Engineering

The seawall of this county was repaired with new-style cement steel bars at a cost of tens of thousands of yuan during the tenure of Director Xu Wei of the Construction Bureau in the 19th year. After the strong wind and rain the year before, the turbulent tide destroyed the piles and dikes. Last year, key repairs were made. Unexpectedly, the cement in sections 245 of the seawall has been washed away in many places. The county government has recently reported the previous situation based on the report of the seawall guards. Xu Mojia, Section Chief of the Third Section of the county government, and technician Yang Lufu drove to the spot for inspection on the 23rd. It was found that the seawall was in danger. After compiling the cost of repairs, the county magistrate submitted it to the Provincial Department of Construction for review and requested funding to prepare for construction.

It is said that he will go to the Taihu Lake to inspect and accept on the 25th.

Wuxi 99

Except for two people who were released, the rest were sentenced to detention. Hangzhou 100

Qing Yu Tang Labor-Capital Dispute Case

The labor-capital dispute case of Qing Yu Tang Chinese Medicine Shop in Hangzhou City has been mediated by the Municipal Chamber of Commerce again and again, but without success. The Construction Department has ordered the municipal government to investigate and deal with the case because the shop assistants have joined the trade union. It is now known that the municipal government has investigated the truth and formulated a solution, which is: (1) Since the shop assistants have joined the trade association, they should withdraw from the trade union; (2) Manager Yu Xiu reinstated; (3) No reduction in salary or dismissal of workers. It is said that the labor and management parties will be ordered to comply. It is said that the labor party has sent representatives to Shanghai to report to the shareholders' meeting and request a meeting to resolve the issue.

Russian Strongman Expresses Submission 101

Shanghai Daily Newspaper Association Telegraphs the Central Political Committee: Redraft the Principles of the Publishing Law and Submit It to the Legislative Yuan for Review 102

The Publishing Law passed by the Legislative Yuan on Wenri is more restrictive than the current law. The press in various places believe that if it is implemented, there will be many difficulties, and it will have a great impact on the press, and even the entire newspaper industry. Therefore, they have gathered together to discuss and request a review. The Shanghai Daily Newspaper Association has telegraphed the National Government, requesting a delay in the promulgation. The original telegram has also been disclosed in various newspapers. The association has also telegraphed the Central Political Committee, the Legislative Yuan, and the Ministry of Interior to make the same request, in order to carry out the proposal of a review. The three telegrams are recorded as follows.

Telegraph to the Central Political Committee

Central Political Review Committee: The Publishing Law revised and passed by the Legislative Yuan on Wenri has a great relationship to culture, but there are many obstacles to its implementation. After deliberation by our association, it is believed that it will be difficult to implement without review. We believe that the principles set by your committee must also be based on the protection of speech. The revisions made by the Legislative Yuan have greatly changed the current law and have added constraints in fact. The various obstacles cannot be detailed in a telegram. In addition to submitting a separate presentation, we would like to telegraph our request first. We respectfully request that your committee re-examine and submit it to the Legislative Yuan for review, in order to conform to the original purpose of supporting the newspaper industry, and to respect the freedom of speech and publication. This is for the public good. Shanghai Daily Newspaper Association.

Telegraph to the Legislative Yuan

Legislative Yuan: The Publishing Law passed by your court on Wenri has a great relationship to culture, but there are many obstacles to its implementation. After deliberation by our association, it is believed that it will be difficult to implement if it is promulgated as it is. We respectfully request your court, based on the spirit of the state's support for the newspaper industry, and in order to respect the freedom of speech and publication, to find a way to revise it. The various difficulties cannot be detailed in a telegram and should be submitted separately for selection. In addition to informing the Central Political Conference and the National Government, we would like to telegraph our request first. We respectfully await your review. Shanghai Daily Newspaper Association.

Telegraph to the Ministry of Interior

Ministry of Interior: The Publishing Law passed by the Legislative Yuan on Wenri has a great relationship to culture, but there are many obstacles to its implementation. After a meeting of our association, it was felt that it would be difficult to implement without review. The Ministry is the competent authority for the newspaper industry, and must also be aware of the crux of the problem, so that it can fulfill its responsibility of protection while suppressing. In addition to submitting a separate presentation to the Central Political Conference and the National Government requesting a review, we would like to telegraph our request first. Shanghai Daily Newspaper Association.

The second district, including Pinding, Xin County, and thirteen other counties, will be surveyed by Jiang Xuekai. The fourth district, including Changzhi, Jin City, and thirteen other counties, will be surveyed by Xie Ze. The fifth district, including Xiaoyi, Hongtong, and fourteen other counties, will be surveyed by Yao Ren. The sixth district, including Linfen, Yangcheng, and fourteen other counties, will be surveyed by Jiang Fu. The seventh district, including Anyi, Yongji, and fourteen other counties, will be surveyed by Yang Zhujun. The eighth district, including Hequ, Baode, and eleven other counties, will be surveyed by Meng Erzang. They are expected to arrive in Shanxi in about three days and will immediately begin their investigations. International Wireless Telephone Expected to Open by Year-End; All Application Devices Now Installed; Trial Calls and Contract Negotiations Underway 108

After the International Telecommunications Bureau of the Ministry of Communications was ordered to prepare for international wireless telephone service, the Wireless Radio Station Engineering Company has completed the installation of all terminal and secret devices. According to Wen Yuqing, Director of the International Telecommunications Bureau, speaking to a reporter from the Xin Xin News Agency, although the international wireless telephone equipment has been installed, they are currently conducting trial calls with Japan, England, and Manila. International calls are quite complex, unlike simple telegrams, so the preparations will take time. The Jingdian Transmission that it would start operating on the 15th of next month may not be so rapid in reality. It is expected that official opening can only be achieved at the end of the year. The Ministry of Communications and the Telecommunications Bureau are separately conducting contract negotiations with various countries regarding the signing of telephone agreements. Detailed methods have been drafted regarding the number of calls, prices, and national zoning methods, and submitted to the Ministry of Communications for review. When official calls begin, they will start in the Zhabei area of Shanghai and gradually expand to the entire city and other locations, such as Nanjing, Beiping, Suzhou, and Wuxi. This international call is similar to making a long-distance call. For example, if Mr. A in Shanghai wants to call Mr. B in Japan, Mr. A only needs to report his telephone number and the address and telephone number to the Telecommunications Bureau. The Telecommunications Bureau will immediately connect the line, allowing Mr. A and Mr. B to speak directly. Therefore, the equipment used is closely related to the telephone bureaus in those locations. In order to simplify and speed up the calling process, the Telecommunications Bureau is striving for thoroughness in all preparations beforehand, to achieve a lasting solution.

Hui Chang and Hua Shun Vessels Collide at Pukou, Sustaining Damage 109

The Hui Chang vessel, belonging to the Shanghai Huitong Company, was transporting goods to Ningbo from Pukou. On the afternoon of the 22nd of this month, at 1:00 PM, when departing from Pukou, it collided with the Hua Shun vessel of the Shanghai Huasheng Shipping Company. The Hui Chang vessel sustained damage to the outer hull of its third hold. The shipowner telegraphed Shanghai to report the incident, stating, "Hui Chang's third hold was breached by the Hua Shun vessel." A subsequent telegram stated, "…" Upon receiving the report, Huitong Company immediately dispatched clerk Lu Huichuan to Nanjing that evening, then on to Pukou, to conduct an on-site inspection and seek a resolution. Lu telegraphed the company, stating that the damage to the Hui Chang vessel caused by the Hua Shun vessel was located on the right side of the third hold, about fifteen feet in length above the waterline, eight feet high, with the deepest indentation about four inches. There was a slight leak below the waterline.

Hua Shun Damaged: The Huasheng Company's Hua Shun vessel also departed from the Pukou dock on the same day. Before the eighth gangway, it collided with the Hui Chang. The captain's report, forwarded to Shanghai by the Huasheng Nanjing agency, stated, in brief, that the Hua Shun vessel was struck head-on by the Huitong Xing Hui Chang vessel when leaving the Pukou dock at 1:02 PM on the 22nd, causing significant damage to the Hua Shun's bow. Detailed circumstances will be reported in full by shipowner Klopp, and will be forwarded to the insurance company as a basis for negotiation.

Temporary Repairs: Because there were no public notaries available in Pukou to verify the leak in the outer hull of the Hui Chang vessel's third hold, Lu Huichuan consulted with and obtained the Hui Chang captain's agreement to temporarily fill the leak with cement, so the vessel could proceed to Ningbo before returning to Shanghai for inspection. Whether there is internal damage to the hull due to the impact will only be clear after inspection in Shanghai. A damage report has been issued to the Huitong Company regarding the damage to the Huasheng vessel's bow for their review.

Notice to All Parties: Yesterday, both Huitong and Huasheng companies sent notices to the China United Ship Insurance Association, which insures their vessels, regarding the collision for their reference. The issue of liability will be determined after both vessels arrive in Shanghai and undergo inspection. It is currently too early to determine who is at fault.

Industrial and Commercial Revival Committee Hosted Press Yesterday Afternoon; Chairman Wang Yansong Delivers Speech Explaining Mission 111

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce's Industrial and Commercial Revival Committee hosted a tea reception for the press at 4:00 PM yesterday. Chairman Wang Yansong delivered a speech explaining the committee's mission and significance. Details are recorded below.

Attendees

Qu Shao Yi, Jin Hua Ting, Sun Dao Sheng of Shen Bao; Shen Ji Cang of Xin Wen Bao; Xue Nong Shan of Shi Shi Xin Bao; He Xi Ya of Chen Bao; Qian Cang Shuo, Guan Jiu An, Wu Zhong Yi of Min Bao; Zhang Zhi Han of Da Mei Wan Bao, and over ten others. Chairman Wang Yansong was accompanied by the committee's Director of General Affairs Yan Esheng, and Executive Director Ren Jinpin, who provided refreshments.

Chairman's Speech

Chairman Wang Yansong said in his speech, "The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, recognizing the severity of the economic panic and the close relationship between industry, commerce, and the economy, deeply understands that in order to resist the attack of the economic panic, it must aid the declining industry and commerce, enabling them to fulfill their duty to save the country and strive for self-reliance. Therefore, the Industrial and Commercial Revival Committee was organized, and I was entrusted with the responsibility of serving as its chairman. I recognize that I am not qualified for the task, but I dare not shrink from difficulty. We have now hired industry leaders and experts to serve as committee members, hoping to cooperate and jointly seek effective remedies. We have now, based on the original proposal, investigated the causes of industrial and commercial decline, studied the principles of revival plans, and formulated a preliminary work process. The investigation team will first conduct investigative work, and then the statistics team will analyze the investigation materials. Then, together with experts, we will study the revival plan and pay attention to training so that assistance from the government and all sectors can be guided. However, to achieve this goal, industry and commerce leaders and owners must cooperate and provide practical assistance. Otherwise, the investigation results may not obtain genuine materials, and the true cause and crux of industrial and commercial decline will not be revealed. I am deeply afraid that even if we encounter a famous doctor with a passion for treating the illness, he will be unable to prescribe medicine because the patient avoids seeking medical attention, or there is a danger of prescribing the wrong medicine. Considering this, I cannot but sincerely expect the public opinion circles to provide strong assistance, guiding colleagues on the one hand, and alerting industrialists and merchants on the other, so that the planning for industrial and commercial revival will not become a mere formality to cope with the environment. Today, the government attaches great importance to the problem of rescuing declining industry and commerce. If there is a concrete and reasonable rescue plan, they will be happy to provide assistance. We must not forget that at the beginning of the 1911 Revolution, the first telegram sent by President Sun Yat-sen from overseas encouraged the people to value industry and commerce. Examining the purpose of various competitions and wars between nations in the world, we find that it lies in the economy. Therefore, whether we want to resist economic attacks or build economic production, we must value industry and commerce, because industry and commerce are weapons for resisting economic attacks and tools for building economic production. Everyone who studies world history today knows that the source of England's wealth and strength lies in its good use of commercial policies. This can be seen in the statistics of England's foreign wars, in which the pursuit of maritime rights and commercial rights is particularly prominent. Although I have not conducted research on the motivation for England's adoption of commercial policies, I speculate that the British must have estimated the results of their initial land productivity and realized that it was insufficient to support the lives of their people, plan their political and military construction, and become strong in the world. Therefore, they vigorously implemented commercial policies to attract foreign economies to support the application of raising the people and repairing political armies. Turning to Japan, we see that its emphasis on commerce seems to have been after the Anglo-Japanese Alliance. Looking at its journey to wealth and strength, it is exactly the same as England. This further proves the importance of the relationship between commerce and national people's livelihood. Today, we all know the pain of national suffering, and everyone has a heart to relieve the country's difficulties. Therefore, industrialists and merchants, for themselves and for the country, should detail the source of the disease in order to seek reasonable assistance, so that each organization can gradually become healthy and can unite with each other to jointly resist economic attacks and strive for the construction of economic production, so that national strength and people's livelihood can benefit from both. Therefore, today, in addition to representing my colleagues to thank you for braving the heat to attend, I also ask you to use the power of public opinion to make industrialists and merchants deeply understand the importance of this investigation and give sincere assistance."

Press Response

He Xiya stood up to respond on behalf of the press, stating that although various parties have paid attention to rescuing industry and commerce in the past, they have only seen words and no effective measures, causing industry and commerce to be deeply suspicious. Now the City Chamber of Commerce has this organization, which starts with investigation, statistics, research, and training, and focuses on practical work. The press is closely related to industry and commerce, so it is very pleased and dares to do its best to assist the committee.

Six Companies Yangtze River Public Tonnage Officially Implemented Today 115

After the six companies' public tonnage contract was established, each company's business will be publicly set a discount to show fairness and to ensure uniformity, so as to avoid private acts such as unauthorized commission release. The agreed-upon discount, according to the results of the representatives' previous discussions, whether shipping to Zhenjiang, Nanjing, Wuhu, Jiujiang, Hankou, and other ports, will be charged at 90% of the tariff rate. In addition to giving a customs broker a 9% commission, the other six companies will all release another 9% commission. Only the Rijii Company requested to release an additional 8.5% commission. The five companies were forced to agree, so the Japanese ships exclusively occupy the advantage.

Problems with Customs Broker Industry

After the implementation of public tonnage, the surface does not涨水脚, but in fact, the original five or six扣佣 released by the individual companies is abolished, and only one stipulated nine deduction commission can be obtained. Only at that time, the six companies each had a special customs broker to report the goods of the bureau, and after the public攤, each other can互装. Last month, there was a claim to organize a customs cooperative, which was later opposed by a general小報关行, and was therefore not realized, and the proposal to limit qualifications was put forward. The method is to investigate the past business of each customs firm, and those with a water foot of 60,000 yuan in a year are first class, those with 30,000 yuan are second class, those with 10,000 yuan are third class, and those with less than 10,000 yuan are unqualified. The general小報关行 heard about it, and was greatly alarmed, which led to the dispute, and the 杂粮帮报关行, etc., due to the lack of procedures to comply, asked to delay for a few days, but the six companies rejected their request.

Shipping Costs After Public Tonnage

From today onwards, the implementation of the public摊, regardless of the upper and lower water cargo, as well as the Yangtze River transit cargo, will be included in the public攤account calculation. The shipping costs agreed upon by the six companies in the public deliberation, roughly from Shanghai 装船, to Hankou and other ports of cargo, based on the number of unit digits, is set to Zhenjiang per ton for six yuan one corner and a half, to Nanjing for eight yuan two corner, to Wuhu for nine yuan two corner, to Jiujiang, and Hankou for eleven yuan six corner and a half, and according to the weight of the jin, to Zhenjiang per ton six yuan five cents, to Nanjing eight yuan five cents, to Wuhu nine yuan five cents, to Jiujiang Hankou for eleven yuan four corner five cents, such as sugar 疋头, cotton yarn, cigarettes, flour, kelp, paper, hardware, cement, and other special rates, and the rest are calculated according to the current tariff.

Determination to Implement from Today

The six companies' river ships and barges have been hired by the company to inspect the ships in batches, and the cargo capacity of each ship is listed as a publicly recognized ton, which is the basis for the public摊standard. Other formalities are also being rushed to completion. The six companies have yesterday telegraphed each port 分行 of Zhen, Ning, Wu, Xun, Han, Sha, Yi, that from the 25th, all the goods loaded and assembled shall be included in the public摊water feet, and all the previous special commissions, rebates, etc., shall be abolished. The specialized accounting office of Thomson, which they hired, also began to work from today.

American Feng Bank Liquidator He Fu Sues for Reimbursement of Gift to Lei Wenzeng; Totaling 400,500 Taels 116

The Shanghai Times reports that He Fu, the liquidator of the American Feng Bank, previously filed a lawsuit with the United States Court in China at the end of June, seeking to recover from Lei Wenzeng, the bank's general manager, a bonus of 135,000 taels granted by the bank's board of directors on January 13, 1932, plus interest. Yesterday, He Fu supplemented his complaint, stating that Lei Wenzeng had received a huge salary before receiving this bonus. From June 1, 1928, to December 31, 1929, he received a monthly salary of 750 yuan. In 1930, he received a monthly salary of 1,000 yuan for the entire year, and at the end of the year, he also received a bonus of 1,800 yuan. Therefore, the bank should not have given Lei Wenzeng a bonus. Lei Wenzeng should immediately return the 135,000 taels he received in fairness and conscience. Moreover, when the board of directors voted to grant the bonus and Lei Wenzeng received it, the bank was on the verge of bankruptcy, and Lei Wenzeng also knew that it was about to go bankrupt. In addition to suing for the 135,000 taels granted to Lei Wenzeng by the American Feng Bank, He Fu is also seeking to recover bonuses of 135,000 taels each granted to Lei Wenzeng by the American East Bank Company and the Puyi Real Estate Company. Lei Wenzeng has not yet filed a statement of defense. Once it is filed, the case will be scheduled for trial.

Requests for Flood Relief from Various Provinces Pour In Like Snowflakes 117

Xu Shiying Reports from Shanghai on Inspection of Hunan Disaster; Says Wang Yilao and Other Senior Generals Should Be Aware: Successive telegrams report the disaster situation, estimated to reach near and far. Your younger brother Yangwu arrived in Changsha, inquired in detail about the severity of the Hunan disaster, and together with Director Yu Jichuan of the Hunan Relief Department, prepared at 7:00 AM to inspect the disaster along the Xiang River, from Xiang Yanliu's Linci Port to Baimasi Hanci Tuan and other places. Most of the dikes had collapsed, and the water had receded several feet in recent days, but the flatlands were still more than ten to twenty feet deep. The water level was higher than in the twentieth year of the Republic. All the crops were submerged, and replanting was impossible. In addition, the disaster situation in lakeside counties such as Yuanjiang, Nanxian, Shou'an Township, Lixian, Changde, and Yiyang was even more severe. As for Cili, Shimen, and Linfeng in western Hunan, it was reported that in early July, they suffered devastating mountain floods, which rose to a depth of forty to fifty feet in an instant, inundating cities and villages, and sweeping away people and livestock. Although the water receded quickly, the disaster was as cruel as that in Tianmen and Hanchuan in Hubei. The Hunan Flood Relief General Association is coordinating relief efforts. Shiying returned to Changsha that evening and transferred to Hubei by special train. Further details will be reported later. Xu Shiying kowtows, Yang.

Reports Received by the Red Swastika Society: The Shanghai General Office of the Society has successively received detailed reports from the Wuhu and Anqing branches regarding the situation of salvaging bodies along the river. The following is a summary to inform those concerned about disaster relief: (1) Respectfully addressed to the United General Office of the Chinese Southeast Branches of the World Red Swastika Society. Kai Rang and Zhi Dao immediately supervised the staff and hired two large rowing boats, carrying salvage equipment, to search along the river. The next morning, they recovered many unidentified corpses at Sihushan and immediately buried them on the spot. Due to the rapid river flow, salvage was difficult. The next day, they hired a new Shengli steamboat, towing several rowing boats, carrying food, coffins, and reed mats. The two branch presidents, Li Kairang and Chen Yuannan, supervised the team members Tang Yuanding and others, as well as more than ten laborers. They set sail at 3:00 PM that afternoon, going up from Datong and down to Dongxi Liangshan, rotating weekly, and doing their best to salvage bodies to prevent the spread of epidemics caused by rotting corpses. A detailed report will be sent again once the ship returns to Wuhu. Wuhu Red Swastika Society kowtows, Ma. (1) Addressed to the Shanghai General Office of the Red Swastika Society. Your electric telegram has been respectfully received and understood. It is our duty to salvage and bury the corpses drowned in the Tianmen and Gucheng floods that are flowing downstream to prevent epidemics, and we will comply. We have immediately notified the boatmen along the river and the life-saving bureaus to salvage any floating corpses coming downstream. This office will provide coffins for burial and reward the corpse-salvaging boatmen according to the number of bodies salvaged. Work is now being carried out separately. This office is also sending personnel to patrol and negotiate at any time. Anqing Office, Ma. Someone like Mr. Bian can be said to be wholeheartedly engaged in relief efforts.

Urgent Telegrams Received by the Sino-Foreign Relief Society: The Sino-Foreign Relief Society on Renlu Road has been receiving reports like snowflakes from the disaster-stricken provinces along the Yellow River and the Yangtze River in recent days. The various tragic situations are unbearable to hear and have been compiled and published in previous reports. Now the Society has received urgent telegrams about the floods in Hubei, Jiangxi, and Shandong, which are specially recorded below: (1) The Joint Association of the Hankou City Chamber of Commerce and the Hubei Provincial Chamber of Commerce telegraphed, saying, "This year, during the summer flood season, continuous rain has caused disasters, and floods have erupted. Recently, the Yangtze and Han rivers have risen simultaneously, and the dikes along the banks have collapsed. In particular, Xiangyang and Fancheng in the upper reaches of the Han River have suffered price reductions. The water is ten feet high, and people are like fish. The Han, Mian, Tian, and Qian areas have become a watery country. Hundreds of thousands of residents have been swept away by the floods and have died. The sight of corpses is heartbreaking. The existing dikes are all in imminent danger and are being reinforced day and night, but it is still difficult to escape danger. Even if they can survive, it will only be a corner of safety, while the disaster is extremely severe, surpassing that of the twentieth year of the Republic. We earnestly request relief." (1) The Xihang Chamber of Commerce of Hubei Zhijiang sent a telegram on behalf of the Zhijiang County, saying, "Zhijiang County is located on the Yangtze River, and the city is the dike. Suddenly, on the song day of this month, mountain floods and torrential rain occurred. Rescue was not possible, resulting in the collapse of the city walls and the inundation of houses. Most of them collapsed, and the goods of merchants and residents were swept away. This unprecedented disaster is heartbreaking. We have long admired your society's concern for the hungry and drowning and earnestly request your swift assistance." (1) The Jiangxi Ruichang County Flood Relief Committee sent a telegram on behalf of the county, saying, "Since late June, continuous rain has been falling in this county, and mountain floods have erupted. The river water has been flowing backward, and it has been rising even more recently, surpassing the disaster situation of the twentieth year of the Republic. People have been climbing onto the roofs to escape by boat, and livestock and halls have been swept away by the waves, cutting off all means of livelihood. Selling children and daughters is common. The cries of refugees are everywhere, and Zheng Xia cannot draw a picture. We humbly request that you bestow your kindness early and distribute relief grain frequently." (1) The representatives of the disaster areas of Shandong Juan, Yun, He, and Ju counties telegraphed, saying, "Since the establishment of the Republic of China, the counties of Juan, Yun, He, and Ju in Shandong have repeatedly suffered Yellow River disasters, especially this year's disaster is the most severe. On the tenth of this month, the Yellow River suddenly breached its banks at Zhuang in Juan County, flowing eastward through the counties of Juan, Yun, He, and Ju. The area it passed through is still the area that was affected by the previous six disasters. The waves are turbulent, and in one day and night, hundreds of miles were flooded. Hundreds of villages have disappeared, with depths exceeding ten feet. The halls have been swept away, and countless people and livestock have drowned. The cries of grief are everywhere, and all the people are victims of the waves. They are suffering from hunger and cold, and the survivors do not know what to do. In addition, continuous rain is adding to the disaster, with torrential rain falling repeatedly. The god of wind is stubborn, often stirring up huge waves. They are exposed to the rain and wind, and their faces are thin and haggard. The situation is tragic and unbearable to witness. If relief is not provided quickly, the millions of disaster victims who have not yet died will all be abandoned in the gullies. We have long known that your society is charitable and cares for the hungry and drowning. We implore you to generously donate funds and jointly undertake this righteous cause, or send personnel to provide relief and save these survivors."

Report Recently Received by the Jinan Provincial Assembly: Guo Fangwu of the Henan Provincial Relief Association recently reported to the Chinese Jinsheng Association that on the morning of July 15, he took a train to Yanshi to inspect the flood disaster. After getting off the train, he went to the temporary office of the county government in Yaocun, north of the city, and met with the county magistrate and relief personnel. Then, together with Chen Ziming, the vice president of the relief association, and Guo Wenrun, the director of the education bureau, he braved the rain to climb the city wall. He walked from the north gate of the city wall to the east gate and then returned to the northwest breach, unable to proceed further. Inside the city, there was a vast expanse of water, which had become a lake. The shallow areas were still more than ten feet deep, and the deep areas were more than twenty feet deep. Compared to the initial rise, the water had receded by more than ten feet. All the houses had collapsed, leaving only a few old brick buildings. The remaining broken walls and wood were scattered everywhere. The stench of human and animal corpses and the smell of rotten buds were nauseating. It was reported that the rise of the Yi and Luo rivers occurred at dawn on the eighth day. The officials and gentry were guarding the south dike, but then they heard that there was danger in the northeast and went to reinforce it, but it was ultimately ineffective. At 1:00 PM, the dike collapsed, and the floodwater entered the city through the two northeast gates. On the southwest side, the dike also collapsed, and the water poured into the city through the four gates. Residents did not have time to escape and either climbed onto the roofs or clung to tree branches, crying for help. The old and weak were swept away, or they were crushed by the collapsing houses, or their corpses floated on the water. According to the household registration, there were 4,364 households in the city, and now 1,207 households are missing, 157 households have been swept away, 67 bodies with names have been found, and hundreds of bodies without names have been found. More than 12,000 refugees have escaped, sleeping in the open air on the crumbling city walls, the moat embankments, and the foothills of Beimang Mountain, without clothes or food, sick and waiting to die. The tragic situation is unbearable to witness. During this flood, County Magistrate Yang of the county led the personnel of various agencies to run around to reinforce the dikes, refusing to leave first, and finally floated out of the water on a piece of wood, calling on the villagers to build rafts to save people. This spirit of sacrifice is admirable. The disaster in the rural areas of the county and in the villages south of the city and in the third and fourth districts is the most severe. In addition, the villages of Dai Su, Luozhuang, Jiong Juanzhen, Xiaoyi Dongzhan, and the villages near the Luo River in Yanshi and Kunlian counties are also extremely tragic. All of this was heard during this trip, but due to road blockages and mud up to the knees, it was not possible to visit all the places. This tragic disaster is unprecedented in a hundred years. In this extremely difficult time of need, all of you great benefactors, if you can vow to provide relief, the number of disaster victims saved will be countless. How can the merits be limited? The blessings will surely be boundless.

The overseas Chinese there are very happy and have recommended Yan Zihuan to propose to the Chamber of Commerce to prepare a national product exhibition. Three methods were decided on the spot: (1) First, prepare for the exhibition, send a letter to the Overseas Chinese United Association and the National National Product United Association to collect new product samples from domestic factories and transport them to Vietnam for public exhibition, so as to arouse the interest of overseas Chinese in adopting national products. (2) When transporting the exhibits, request the resident government to specify the tax rate for each item and postpone taxation. After the exhibition, those suitable for sale in Vietnam will be taxed according to the tax rate. (3) For various national products, if it is considered that they can be promoted in Vietnam, a large-scale national product company should be organized immediately to increase sales strength. They are currently discussing methods with Wang Hanqiang and others from the National Product Maintenance Association.

The Directorate General of Posts Submits to the Ministry to Suspend the Mailing of Sugar Powder and Coffee Essence; Although Various Items Have Been Tested and Found to Be Non-Toxic, They Are Materials for Preparing Drugs 121

The Directorate General of Posts, due to the fact that parcels of sugar powder, coffee essence, caffeine, lactose, etc., sent from Shanghai to the interior have been detained by local governments from time to time, has specially requested the Ministry of Communications to temporarily suspend the mailing of the above-mentioned parcels. The original report stated, "Regarding the case of mailing parcels of sugar powder, coffee essence, etc., in the nineteenth year of the Republic of China, the Zhejiang and Henan Management Bureaus successively reported that local authorities had confiscated parcels of sugar powder, which were raw materials for manufacturing the drug 'Hongwan,' and had confiscated them. Samples were sent to the Shanghai Management Bureau for transfer to the Customs for testing, and they were found not to contain any toxic substances and were not on the list of prohibited items. It was then reported and instructed that since the Customs had tested and proved that they did not contain toxic substances, they should be allowed to be received and mailed as usual for the convenience of merchants, and the governments of Zhejiang and Henan provinces should be notified to check and comply. In the tenth year of the same year, it was reported by the Shanxi Management Bureau that parcels of saccharin powder in the Shanxi area were detained in accordance with the measures of the Shanxi Provincial Government to prohibit the trafficking and manufacturing of 'Jindan' raw materials. The Ministry then consulted the Opium Prohibition Committee as to whether this saccharin powder was a raw material for manufacturing drugs and whether it should be allowed to be mailed. Later, it was instructed to send a letter from the Opium Prohibition Committee to the Ministry of Interior's Health Department for delivery to the Central Hygiene Laboratory for testing. According to the report, the test results showed that it did not contain drugs. The main ingredients of 'Jindan' and 'Baiwan' were morphine, cocaine, heroin, and other narcotics. Saccharin starch was a shaping drug and could be dispensable. If morphine, cocaine, heroin, etc., can be completely banned from import, then saccharin starch can be banned without prohibition. Please check and order the relevant authorities to be notified. In October of the twenty-second year, it was reported by the Henan Management Bureau that a parcel sent from Shanghai to Anyang was detained by the Anyang County Government as a prohibited item. The Shanghai Management Bureau was immediately ordered to investigate and found that it was sent by the Da Zhongxi Pharmacy, containing coffee essence. According to the Customs, coffee essence is a Western medicine material, and the regulations are for treating cold and fever. They are not on the list of prohibited items. The bureau was immediately ordered to notify the relevant authorities. Subsequently, it was reported that the Anyang County Government had also sent it to the County Hospital for testing and found that it did not contain any toxic substances. It was returned to the recipient in full. Therefore, the post office has been receiving and mailing parcels of saccharin and coffee essence as usual. Recently, it has been reported by the Henan Management Bureau that in the twenty-third year, eleven parcels of lactose sent from Tianjin to Wuji Town, Wu'an, were confiscated by the Wu'an County Government. In addition, several parcels of coffee essence sent from Shanghai to Anyang were confiscated by the Anyang County Government. Recently, the Anyang County Government detained a cash-on-delivery parcel sent from Shanghai to Anyang. After inquiry, it was said that it contained two tubes of 'Jianqiang Kui' silver, two tubes of coffee essence, three bottles of 'Shidine,' and five bottles of 'Nuo Jiaco Yin,' which were all necessary for compounding drugs. Later, a letter was received stating that the Henan Provincial Government had instructed that they should be confiscated and burned. They hoped for investigation and so on. The bureau has always paid great attention to investigating and prohibiting the mailing of prohibited items. If there are suspicious parcels, the court or the competent authorities are notified at any time to investigate and verify them. All parcels of coffee essence, caffeine, lactose, etc., are inspected and released by the Tianjin and Shanghai Customs because they are not prohibited items. When they are sent to this area, the authorities consider them to be raw materials for manufacturing drugs and detain them all. Now that the Henan Provincial Government has ordered their confiscation, can the bureaus of Tianjin and Shanghai be instructed to stop receiving and mailing coffee essence, lactose, etc., to Henan? Please review and approve the handling. Based on this, the post office has repeatedly ordered the prohibition of illegal merchants from mailing prohibited items. If there are suspicious parcels, the local competent authorities are notified for verification. The post office and the local authorities belong to the same national agency. If there are relevant special items, they should be handled uniformly. However, the Customs considers that the sugar powder, coffee essence, etc., do not contain any toxic substances, so the post office allows them to be received and mailed. Now the Henan Provincial Government considers them to be raw materials for manufacturing drugs and has repeatedly detained them. If this situation continues to be ambiguous, not only will it be difficult to handle, but it will also easily cause misunderstandings, and the people will also feel inconvenienced. Therefore, it is proposed to notify all districts that the receipt and mailing of parcels of sugar powder, coffee essence, caffeine, lactose, and regulations will be temporarily suspended. It is also proposed to request the ministry to consult the Henan Provincial Government to clarify the situation and to request that if there are any matters related to mailing in the future, the ministry should be consulted first for review and handling in order to avoid ambiguity in the methods. It is reported that the Ministry of Communications has approved the bureau to issue an order to its subordinates to temporarily prohibit the mailing of saccharin and coffee essence, etc. When the situation in various places allows for the ban to be lifted, the receipt and mailing will be resumed. The regulations, since they are medicines for treating diseases, should be excluded and not on the list of prohibited items.

Yesterday Was "Great Heat": Japanese Residents Superstitiously Eat Eel 129

According to the Shanghai Japanese Daily, the 24th was the "Great Heat" festival, which the Japanese call "Doyo no Ushi no Hi." On this day, according to Japanese custom, everyone should eat eel, meaning that after eating eel on the "Great Heat" day, they can avoid colds and other illnesses this year. This superstition is prevalent throughout Japan, so yesterday, Japanese restaurants in this city prepared large quantities of eel to supply customers. The eel that best suits the taste of Japanese residents is Niigata eel. In recent days, eel vendors in various small vegetable markets have seen their profits multiply.
