Catching Mosquitoes Leads to Burial in Flames: The Family of Gu Miaojin is Ruined 131

Gu Miaojin, a mason from Liujiabang Village, Zhanghuabang, Wusong, was considered middle class. The night before last, he attended a banquet with friends and returned home at dusk, already intoxicated. He fell asleep immediately. At midnight, his wife suddenly got up to catch mosquitoes, lighting a kerosene lamp for light. She was careless and accidentally knocked over the kerosene lamp onto the bed curtains. The curtains immediately caught fire, and flames soared. Gu woke up from his dream and helped his wife put out the fire. However, the fire intensified due to the wind, and soon it pierced the roof and became uncontrollable. Gu had to escape from the fire, fortunately unharmed. His wife, being a woman, also escaped from the house, but she was burned all over her body. Five rooms of their own house were burned down, fortunately not affecting the neighbors. All their belongings were reduced to ashes. Yesterday, Gu took his wife to the Wusong Health Hospital for treatment, but she died due to the fire attacking her heart and lungs. It is tragic that catching mosquitoes led to family ruin.

Blood and Sweat Money Swindled: Zhuang Huaiyou is Indeed Pitiful; How Can Qi Xinming Be So Heartless? 132

Zhuang Huaiyou, a 42-year-old from Yizhou, Shandong, left his hometown in his youth to work in Hong Kong, engaged in mountain opening and road construction for 26 years. He saved 300 yuan of hard-earned money and took a ship from Hong Kong back to his hometown. He arrived in Shanghai on the 3rd of this month. Zhuang, unfamiliar with Shanghai, wanted to stay in a hotel. While he was hesitating on the ship, Qi Xinming (28 years old), a native of Anhui who worked as a hotel tout for the Guangtailai Hotel at 107 Avenue Edward VII in the French Concession, approached Zhuang and led him to the Guangtailai Hotel, where he booked room 207. Qi saw that Zhuang was a rustic and ignorant fellow, and knowing that Zhuang had a large sum of money, he harbored malicious intentions. He pretended to be helpful and colluded with an accomplice, Mr. Jia, instructing Zhuang to take 200 yuan in cash and go with Mr. Jia to a bank to exchange it for Shandong Province general currency, saying that this would avoid exchange losses when he arrived in Shandong. Zhuang believed him and followed Mr. Jia with the money to the front of a foreign firm on the Bund. Mr. Jia told Zhuang that there were "red-headed devils" (foreigners) guarding the entrance of the bank who would not allow poorly dressed people to enter, so he could give the money to Mr. Jia to exchange it for him. Zhuang, unaware of the deception, handed over the money and watched Mr. Jia enter the bank. He waited outside for several hours, but Mr. Jia did not come out. Zhuang inquired inside but found no clues. He returned to the Guangtailai Hotel dejectedly and confronted Qi Xinming. However, Qi flatly denied introducing an acquaintance to exchange the money. Zhuang, struck by this, was depressed all day. Qi, knowing that Zhuang still had money, invited Zhuang to stay at his home to save money. Zhuang, still unaware of the scheme, rashly agreed. They went to Qi's home upstairs at 87 Xixinqiao Street. At the same time, Qi asked Zhuang for 80 yuan as capital for doing petty trading in other places, saying that any profits would be shared. Zhuang agreed and gave Qi the money. After a few days, Qi gave Zhuang 29 yuan, saying it was the profit from the trading. Meanwhile, Qi secretly incited hooligans to threaten Zhuang, forcing him to leave Shanghai and wanting to rob Zhuang of his silver dollars. Zhuang refused to yield and continued to stay at Qi's home, gradually pawning his belongings. Qi then falsely claimed to Zhuang that the capital he had given him had been confiscated by the customs. As a result, the two had a quarrel. On the 16th of this month, both parties were taken to the French Concession police station. After questioning by the police chief, Qi was arrested for fraud and ordered to be detained. The next day, he was sent to the Special Second Court. After hearing the case, Judge Dong Qiming of the Special Second Court continued the trial in the Eighth Criminal Court yesterday morning. Police lawyer Yuan Jiahong presented the case and prosecuted Qi for fraud. The plaintiff, Zhuang Huaiyou, recounted the circumstances of the fraud and hired a lawyer to file a private lawsuit. Detective Wang Yamin then reported the results of the investigation. Qi Xinming confessed that he only took 80 yuan from Zhuang to trade silver dollars in Hong Kong for profit, but it was confiscated by the customs and there was no fraud of 200 yuan. Zhou Guiting, the second landlord of the defendant, testified that he only knew that Wang and Qi were arguing about money. The court reviewed the testimonies and ordered a further hearing on the 27th, as it was still necessary to summon witnesses. The defendant was returned to custody.

Republic of China Year 22 Homicide Case Solved Yesterday: Yao Gonglin Admits Without Reservation 133

In October of the 22nd year of the Republic of China, a gangster named Ji A'gen, residing in Youyuli, Gonghe Road, Zhabei, was attacked in the early morning by enemies wielding axes and pistols, suffering injuries to his shoulders, back, hands, and feet, and was shot in the tip of his nose and killed. The murderer fled and was not apprehended. Unexpectedly, the murderer, Yao Gonglin, was spotted in front of the Citibank building on Jiujiang Road yesterday noon by the deceased's wife, Ji Wangshi. Wang secretly informed the constable on duty there, who arrested him and took him to the Central Patrol Station. After questioning by the police chief, as the case occurred within the jurisdiction of the Zhabei Xinzha Branch, he called the branch to send personnel to take custody. Upon receiving the report, Chief Ruan of the branch immediately ordered Detective Squad Leader Bao Ziying to send Deputy Squad Leader Liu Changpei and Detective Mao Gongzhao to the Central Patrol Station to take Yao Gonglin into custody. Yao confessed that he was 27 years old, from Zhenjiang, and was currently working as a copper worker's assistant in a boiler room in the Citibank building on Erma Road. He admitted that he and several accomplices killed Ji A'gen with axes and pistols on the 24th day of the eighth lunar month in the 22nd year of the Republic of China (i.e., October in the Gregorian calendar). He also stated that he was instructed by someone to do so, and they originally planned to cut off one of Ji's hands or feet, but the situation became deadlocked, so they killed him. After the incident, he fled to the Kunshan County Public Security Bureau to serve as a detective, etc. He also confessed to the names of several accomplices. The Detective Squad sent personnel to arrest them separately, but the accomplices had already fled upon hearing the news. Therefore, the Detective Squad is currently conducting a strict investigation.

Ministry of Railways Broadcasts Standard Time This Morning, Transmitting to All Railway Bureaus for Compliance 136

The Ministry of Railways, due to discrepancies in the train schedules of various railway lines, which have a significant impact on the railway transport, has decided to adopt the Central Standard Time for broadcasting to all railway lines for compliance, in order to ensure that all railway schedules are consistent. It is reported that this measure will be officially implemented starting today, with the Ministry of Railways broadcasting to all railway bureaus, and then the railway bureaus transmitting to all stations, so that the schedules of all domestic railway lines are completely consistent. The broadcasting time is from 8:55 AM to 9:05 AM every day. According to spokespersons of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administrations, the measure has been ordered to be followed by all stations of the bureau. Several test broadcasts have been conducted recently, and the results have been very good. Other railway stations have also made similar preparations and do not need to install additional radio stations.

Russian Merchant "Oil Everywhere" Company in Litigation with "Guanghua Kerosene" Company: Person in Charge of the Mainland Bank Talks About the Case 143

Regarding the case of litigation between the Russian merchant "Oil Everywhere" Company and the "Guanghua Kerosene" Company, according to the person in charge of the Mainland Bank, Guanghua Kerosene Company has always been involved in the transportation and sale of Russian kerosene, and its business has been quite developed. In November of last year, after renegotiating the purchase and sale contract with "Oil Everywhere", it had already ordered several batches without any objections. However, due to extreme economic decline and rural bankruptcy, sales sharply decreased. Moreover, when the contract was renegotiated, Guanghua claimed that the color and quality of the oil purchased from "Oil Everywhere" did not comply with the contract, resulting in further stagnation in sales. Therefore, it was difficult to fulfill the contract quota. Guanghua Company had repeatedly negotiated with "Oil Everywhere", and Mr. Odyn, the former representative of "Oil Everywhere" stationed in Shanghai who signed the contract at the time, also acknowledged that the current decline in the oil market was a real situation. When he left Shanghai to return to Moscow, he promised to discuss a method to appropriately reduce the quota with his head office, and repeatedly stated that "Oil Everywhere" would cooperate with Guanghua to promote sales and would not penalize Guanghua. Therefore, Guanghua Company continued to make efforts to promote sales and waited for Mr. Odyn's response. Unexpectedly, after Mr. Odyn left, there was no news for a long time. Recently, "Oil Everywhere" suddenly changed its attitude, completely denying the previous negotiations with Guanghua, and directly claimed that Guanghua Company had breached the contract, demanding that Guanghua pay a penalty of 100,000 yuan, and requiring the bank, as Guanghua's guarantor, to pay on its behalf. It was the case that when "Oil Everywhere" and Guanghua renegotiated the contract, the usual bank guarantee was required. Our bank and the Guohuo, Guohua, and Shanghai banks had existing joint business relationships with Guanghua, such as opening letters of credit, overdrafts, etc. Therefore, the Guohuo, Guohua, Shanghai, and our bank jointly guaranteed the contract, and our bank represented them in signing the guarantee letter, stipulating a guarantee liability limited to 200,000 yuan. At the same time, the bank obtained full collateral from Guanghua to prepare for any eventuality. Therefore, the bank could readily disburse the funds at any time. However, because Guanghua itself now denies having breached the contract, and its shareholders raised objections to the renegotiated contract and successively came to the bank requesting a halt to the payment, the bank could not ignore Guanghua's interests and pay the penalty. This caused the lawsuit filed by "Oil Everywhere". In short, since this case has already gone to litigation, it must await the court's judgment. The key point lies in the dispute between Guanghua and "Oil Everywhere". After the court's trial and judgment, the question of whether Guanghua should pay the penalty can be resolved at the same time. Since this case occurred, the bank has been in a third-party position and has no vested interest in it. However, it seems to be more harmful than beneficial to "Oil Everywhere"'s Far East market. (Central News Agency)

New Life Movement Association Streamlines Shipping, Appoints Liu Hongsheng as Instructor, Gradually Reforms the Bad Habits of Servants, Issues Revised Plan for Streamlining China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Servants 144

The Central News Agency reports that the Nanchang New Life Movement Promotion Association, in order to streamline shipping and make the servants of various ships aware of the implementation of the New Life Movement, specially appointed Liu Hongsheng as the instructor for the New Life Movement in shipping, and ordered him to draft a plan for implementation. Mr. Liu immediately expressed his acceptance and drafted a plan, which was submitted to the New Life Movement Association for review and decision. Yesterday, the New Life Movement Association revised the plan and sent it down, and dispatched the association's cadre and secretary, Yan Baohang, to assist in the implementation. Mr. Yan is expected to arrive in Shanghai today. The association also sent a letter to the Ministry of Communications, instructing various shipping companies to cooperate in handling the matter, and sent a letter to the Central People's Movement Committee, instructing the Shanghai Branch of the Chinese Seamen's Union to cooperate in the implementation, in order to achieve practical results in streamlining. It is learned that Mr. Yan will start the implementation immediately after arriving in Shanghai, starting with the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and then extending to other private shipping companies. The revised plan of the Association is excerpted below:

Plan for Streamlining China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Servants

1. Purpose: To promote the New Life Movement, so that the servants of various ships know how to observe discipline, be polite, be sanitary, and fulfill their duties, so that all ships have an orderly appearance.

2. Current situation: (A) The number of servants on various ships of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company is excessive. The New Jiangtian Ship has as many as 270 servants on the main shift. Other river ships, such as the first-class Jiangshun, Jianghua, Jiangxin, and Jiang'an ships, each have more than 110 to 150 servants. Second-class ships, such as the Jianguo, Jiangda, and Jiangjing, have around 100 servants. Ocean liners, such as the Xin Mingda, have more than 60 servants, while other ships have less than 40 servants. (B) Because of the large number of people and the lack of salaries, extortion for tips, privately carrying passengers, and selling drugs are common occurrences. (C) The servants of various ships lack the knowledge and skills of service and lack the necessary management, so there is no way to talk about sanitation, etiquette, or discipline.

3. Reasonable system: (A) The implementation of a reasonable system starts with reducing the number of servants. Based on the number of passenger seats and the complexity of the business, a standard quota should be set, and the excess number should be eliminated or other remedies sought. (B) The servants of various ships should be directly hired and managed by the company, and service rules should be stipulated and strictly enforced by the heads of each ship. The tipping system should be changed to a salary system, and tips should not be collected. (C) The servants of various ships must wear uniforms and badges in order to work on the ship.

4. Implementation methods: (A) Establish a New Life Training Class for Servants, and rotate the servants of various ships to the shore for training, teaching them the knowledge and skills of service that they should have, and cultivating their character to meet the requirements of the New Life Movement. (B) The training course includes: (A) Military training, (B) New Life Knowledge, (C) Service Common Sense, (D) Spiritual Admonition, (E) Others (Mandarin, dialect, letters, etc.). (C) Those who pass the examination upon completion of the training will be given a certificate for employment. Those who do not pass will be given severance pay. If the number of qualified servants exceeds the actual number needed, a rotational service method will be stipulated in advance to provide relief. (D) The servants of various ships should gradually change to a salary system, and tips should not be collected. Before the salary system is implemented, the maximum amount of tips should be stipulated, and passengers should be free to give rewards without extortion. (E) The business department of each ship should be managed by a full-time employee. The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company should introduce business directors for each ship who are responsible for the employment of servants.

5. The New Life Training Class for Servants is guided by the New Life Movement Promotion Association, organized by the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, and assisted by the Seamen's Union.

Hua Inspector Feng Zhiming, Liu Shaokui, and Detective Wu Hanzhang of the General Inspectorate of the Public Concession Police apprehended nine suspects including Zhang Xueyuan, Li Yucai, and Bao Xuewen in a large-scale counterfeit currency operation at No. 806 Zhoujiazui Road on the morning of the 9th of this month. Special Tribunal

Counterfeit Currency Ring

Health Bureau to Conduct Registration of Maternity Patients and Prevent Hospital Fraudulent Practices 147

Li Ting'an, the director of the Municipal Health Bureau, has specially ordered You Jihua, the director of the Shanghai South District Health Office, to prepare everything for public health, maternal and infant health, and registration of maternity patients. The following is a breakdown of the situation as learned by a National Press reporter:

Implementation of Maternal and Infant Health

It is unknown how many women are sacrificed in China because of childbirth by old-fashioned midwives. Every time a midwife helps deliver a child, she uses broken porcelain and broken glass and iron scissors to cut the baby's umbilical cord, with no knowledge of disinfection methods. There is no midwifery technique and no scientific knowledge, so infants often develop umbilical cord wind, (namely tetanus, commonly known as seven-day wind), and die. There is no way to handle the after-childbirth and baby-care measures, so mothers are at risk of developing "postpartum fever." Director Li believes that this is especially true in Shanghai, and the consequences would be dire if this continues. He issued a special order yesterday to You Jihua, the director of the Shanghai South District Health Office, to implement maternal and infant health care in order to avoid the sacrifice of mothers and infants and to ensure their safety.

Conducting Maternity Patient Registration

In order to protect the safety of mothers and babies, the Municipal Health Bureau will conduct maternity registration in the Shanghai South District Health Office on Linqin Road in Nanshi, and will formulate regulations and various forms. All pregnant women who are more than five months pregnant can go to the office to obtain a registration form, fill it out and submit it to the office for record. There will be specialists to guide the diet and living arrangements and the maintenance method of pregnancy, and to regularly check whether there is any abnormality in the baby's position. At the same time, there will be considerable corrections to the daily movements of pregnant women. According to You Jihua, the director of the Shanghai South District Health Office, who spoke to the National Press reporter, the hospital plans to cooperate with Nanshi Shanghai Public Hospital to implement maternal and infant health care, but the formalities for maternity registration are still being prepared, and it will be implemented in about a month.

Preventing False Name Fraud

Recently, a number of obstetrical hospitals in the city have been publishing advertisements in various newspapers, and their delivery prices are prominently displayed as being cheap, but many citizens have been deceived. Although scientific methods are also used for delivery, apart from the delivery fee, they will fraudulently establish various expenses, such as injection of labor-inducing drugs, hemostatic drugs, blood tonic drugs, and cardiotonic drugs, which results in a considerable amount of money, which puts a heavy burden on the pregnant woman's economy. Therefore, the bureau will take measures to prevent the above-mentioned obstetrical hospitals from defrauding patients.

Case of Judge's Dereliction of Duty Transferred to Shanghai for Trial 148

When Feng Jiasheng, a prosecutor of the Minhou District Court in Fujian, was on duty, he handled a case in which Chen, the party concerned, was detained even though he should not have been detained, causing Chen to become ill in detention and die without medical treatment. Chen's family was deeply dissatisfied and charged Feng Jiasheng with causing death due to dereliction of duty to the Fujian High Court, which transferred jurisdiction to the Shanghai District Court. A public prosecution was filed based on the facts, and a public trial should be held soon.

License Fees for Rickshaws and Handcarts Temporarily Suspended from Increase; Original Intention of Tax Increase Not Entirely Financial 149

Since the Municipal Council decided to increase the license fees for rickshaws and handcarts in the Public Concession, it has been repeatedly protested and opposed. The Finance Committee of the Municipal Council has repeatedly considered this matter, and recently decided that the license fees should be temporarily suspended from being increased. However, a precise investigation of the position of these human-powered carts in traffic is still necessary in order to determine future policies. It is reported that the board of directors of the Municipal Council has adopted the Finance Committee's recommendation.

The tax increase for rickshaws and handcarts was based on the quota of various taxes and license fees of the Municipal Council passed at the Western Taxpayers' Annual Meeting in the spring of this year, and should have been implemented from July 1 this year. Subsequently, the industry submitted a request to withdraw the order, taking into account the difficulties of commerce, and also requested the Chinese Taxpayers' Association to appeal on its behalf. The Municipal Council then had a plan to postpone the increase. However, the increase in taxes was not entirely for financial reasons. The so-called rickshaws are originally small carts for transporting goods at the pier, which are used exclusively for cargo warehouses and stations at the pier, with a load limit of 500 pounds. However, over time, abuses have arisen. These carts are now all over the city's streets, and the load limit has been exceeded, with many weighing up to 1,000 pounds. As a result, the road surface is often damaged when they travel on the road. After discussion by the heads of various departments in the Municipal Council, it was decided to increase the license fees in order to limit them, and the license stipulated that the load must not exceed 300 pounds. Now that the increase in license fees has had to be postponed due to the opposition of the industry, there is still room for discussion on the position of these vehicles in traffic. According to the opinion expressed by the Finance Committee during the discussion, on the one hand, the number of licenses for existing vehicles must be limited, and on the other hand, other methods must be found to ban them. Some also suggested that rickshaws should be equipped with rubber wheels. Others said that after rickshaws are equipped with rubber wheels, the bureau can return one-third of the license fees to show preferential treatment. However, whether the car owners have the financial resources to do so is still questionable. As a result, in addition to the postponement of the increase in license fees, the traffic issue will be discussed after a thorough investigation.

Xin Sheng News Agency reports that after the committee of the Municipal Council resolved to postpone the tax increase for rickshaws and handcarts, the board of directors held a meeting yesterday to approve the postponement of the increase in license fees. The committee also suggested that the board of directors restrict the current number in order to ban them. It is advocated that rickshaws be converted to rubber tires to protect the road surface. After the car owners install rubber wheels, all tax amounts will be reduced by one-third, and the load is limited to 500 pounds. After discussion by the board of directors yesterday, it was decided to first investigate the total number of vehicles and then discuss it. The Mutual Aid Association for the two industries will hold an establishment meeting at the original site of New World at 2:00 p.m. today.

The photo on the right is a group photo of students from the Motor Vehicle Mechanic Training Institute visiting the Li Han Automobile Company at the roof test track (photographed by Xu Tianzhang).

Lumber Industry Group Opposes Categorized Business Licenses; Submits Petition to Chinese Taxpayers' Association for Just Representation 151

The lumber industry in the French Concession opposes the French Municipal Council's unprovoked collection of categorized business licenses and an investigation fee of ten yuan, which is difficult to bear in the current depressed market. Yesterday, they submitted a joint petition to the French Concession Chinese Taxpayers' Association for just representation. The Lumber Industry Trade Association also sent a letter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, requesting the municipal government to negotiate with the French Party Bureau. The Xin Xin News Agency has compiled the following details:

Group Opposition

The lumber industry submitted a joint petition to the French Concession Chinese Taxpayers' Association for just representation yesterday in order to understand the difficulties of commerce. The original letter reads, "To whom it may concern, we are now informed that the Chinese and Westerners from the French Concession Public Affairs Bureau are carrying a notice from the bureau's Categorized Business Department, claiming that we should immediately donate and obtain a categorized business hygiene license from the bureau and pay an examination fee of two yuan and ten yuan, which is shocking. We have been open for many years, and there has never been such a donation certificate. In February of the year before last, the bureau issued a notice to us to donate and obtain a license, and we sent a letter to your association to negotiate with the French Public Affairs Bureau. Subsequently, we received a letter from the bureau stating that, with the exception of the construction industry, donation certificates could be exempted. The question of whether our industry should donate a certificate is unnecessary to elaborate on. Now the Public Affairs Bureau is fickle and has issued a donation certificate again after two years. It is unfortunate that the lack of fairness in public affairs is regrettable for the taxpayers in the concession. At this time, the market is extremely depressed, and the impact on our industry is even greater than that of other industries. If we increase the donation again, we will be unable to bear it. Therefore, we jointly send this letter to your association, requesting that you forward a letter to the French Public Affairs Bureau to negotiate and cancel the donation certificate."

Request for Just Representation

The Lumber Industry Trade Association of the Lumber Market received letters from members such as Yin Ji, Tong Xing, Zheng Da, etc., stating that the French Municipal Council unreasonably increased taxes and requested a transfer to the French authorities for negotiation. After learning of the situation, the association immediately sent a letter to the Chinese Taxpayers' Association, which read: "To whom it may concern, we now received a letter from lumber companies such as Bin Ji, Mao Sheng, Cheng Da, Tong Xing, Fu Xing, Li Da, He Tai, Li Xing, Hou Da, and Zheng Da, stating that four people from the Categorized Business Department of the French Concession Public Affairs Bureau came to the number and claimed that, starting from today, they should donate and obtain a categorized business hygiene license from the Public Affairs Bureau and pay an examination fee of ten yuan, which is unbearable in the current depression of all industries. According to the increase in taxes, government orders must be used as a measure, even within the concession, the procedure must be approved by your association. Now the bureau has rashly levied taxes, which is inconsistent with the law. Especially when commerce is in decline, it should be maintained and not exploited in order to revitalize the market. In addition to sending a letter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to transfer to the municipal government for negotiation, we especially send a letter to your association to help in the interest of justice in order to revive commerce.

Twins Die Horribly with Mother 155

Xia Agui, a boatman in his twenties, from Wusong Wenzaobang, is currently working as a sailor on the Tongchongban shipping line. His wife, Ms. Li, is about the same age as Agui and had given birth once, but died. She became pregnant again recently, and on the morning of the 18th of this month, she suddenly had abdominal pain, and then gave birth to a boy, who died as soon as he landed. Unexpectedly, the abdominal pain continued after delivery, and a midwife found that there was another child in Ms. Li's abdomen, which was not easy to deliver for a while. Therefore, with the consent of the woman who was giving birth, the child was cut off surgically, but had already died for a long time, and the skin and flesh had become putrid. Ms. Li was physically weak after giving birth, and felt that both of her children had died, so she could not help but feel very sad. She died yesterday morning after treatment failed, which is truly a tragic event. Now Agui's uncle, Xia Xingyuan, is preparing a coffin for burial on his behalf.

The Two Courts Burn Publications and Drugs in Stages - Reactionary Publications and Various Drugs Have Been Approved by the Ministry for Public Burning 169

Publications: The Second Branch of the Jiangsu Higher Court will routinely collect and burn the publications confiscated in cases involving harming the Republic of China after the case is finalized. The publications that the court has accumulated and should be burned, from October of last year to June of this year, include "The Decameron," "The First Five-Year Plan," "Diary on Horseback," "The End of Winter," and reactionary propaganda leaflets, etc., in a large number. The court's President Shen and Chief Prosecutor Zheng Lunxian jointly submitted a report to the Ministry of Judicial Administration and were instructed to allow the burning. It has been decided that the public burning will take place at 11:00 AM on the 27th of this month. The burning location will still be the open space in the Yizhong Cemetery of Bao'an Hall on the south side of the court. In addition to sending letters to various party, government, military, police, and legal groups such as the Shanghai Municipal Council Lawyers Association, inviting them to send representatives to supervise the burning, Shen and Zheng have also informed the public.

Drugs: The red pills, opium, and various toxic substances confiscated in drug cases by the First Special District Local Court are routinely submitted to the Ministry of Judicial Administration for approval and public burning every three months to eliminate drug fumes. Since its implementation, it has been held twenty times. The court's President Guo and Chief Prosecutor Xiang, considering that there are a considerable number of toxic substances accumulated for burning from March to June of this year, followed the usual practice of submitting a report to the Ministry and were instructed to publicly burn the toxic substances that have been finalized in accordance with the law. Guo and Xiang have scheduled the twenty-first public drug burning at 3:00 PM on the 31st of this month, still at the Yizhong Cemetery of Bao'an Hall on North Zhejiang Road on the south side of the court. In addition to sending letters to various agencies and legal groups, inviting them to send representatives to supervise the event, the public has also been informed.

Davis Cup Inter-Zone Final - United States Wins the Challenge Round - Allison Wins Three Straight Sets Against Henkel - United States Eliminates Germany 3-1 170

(London, 24th - Reuters) In the Davis Cup Inter-Zone Final, the United States eliminated Germany 3-1, winning the challenge round. They will compete against Great Britain for the challenge round. In today's third singles match, Allison of the United States defeated Henkel of Germany in three straight sets. In total, the United States eliminated Germany by a score of three to one. The singles match between Budge and Kramm is no longer relevant.

United States Wins Doubles Against Germany - Fierce Battle Decided After Five Sets - American Team Escapes Death 171

(London, 23rd - Reuters) In the Davis Cup Inter-Zone Final between Germany and the United States, the American team of Allison and Van Ryn, considered one of the strongest doubles teams in the world, was almost defeated by the German team of Kramm and Lundt. The American team barely survived a hard fight. The results are as follows:

Unless there are unexpected changes in tomorrow's reversed singles matches, the United States should win the challenge round. Although Budge's chances of winning against Kramm are slim, Allison should be able to defeat Henkel.

From Beginning to End

The battle was very fierce. Germany needed only one point to win the whole match five times - twice in the fourth set and three times in the fifth set. Fortunately, the American team fought hard and barely escaped.

First Set

The Germans were unstoppable. Kramm's serves repeatedly scored points, and he and Lundt often had opportunities to kill the ball at the net. This set ended in just nineteen minutes, with Germany winning 6-3.

Second Set

Allison and Van Ryn showed their skills at the net, also winning the second set 6-3. It only took twelve minutes.

Third Set

The Germans took a 5-2 lead. The Americans desperately chased to 5-5, but the Germans still won 7-5.

Fourth Set

In the tenth game, the Germans needed only one point to win twice. Fortunately, Allison's net interceptions saved the day.

Fifth Set

The most thrilling. Allison and Van Ryn took a 4-1 lead. Kramm and Lundt won four games in a row, taking a 5-4 lead. Three times, the Germans needed only one point to win. In the end, the Americans managed to salvage the situation, winning 8-6.

(2) It was decided to hold the preliminary selection on August 2nd at the Zhongqing pool. (3) Two people will be selected for each event, and one person for the 800-yard event. (4) The selected athletes will practice at the Zhongqing pool every day, and Mr. Peng Sanmei will be hired as the coach. (5) Li Rixin and Yu Binqi will be hired as managers. (6) The official list of the Chinese team must be submitted to the West YMCA by August 9th. (7) Practice at the West YMCA swimming pool about three times before the official competition. The time will be determined separately. The meeting adjourned at 9:30.

Zhongqing and West YMCA Swimming Confrontation 179

At 8:30 PM on the 27th at the West YMCA Pool

The Zhongqing swimming team will hold a friendly match against the West YMCA at the West YMCA pool the day after tomorrow (Saturday). A water polo match will also be held after the competition. The confrontation events include the 50-yard freestyle, 100-yard freestyle, 400-yard freestyle, 100-yard breaststroke, 100-yard backstroke, and three-style relay race. There will also be a water polo match. Tickets are divided into two types: upstairs and downstairs. Upstairs is 30 cents, and downstairs is 60 cents. Zhongqing also believes that this competition has an international nature, so the Aviation Association's invitation to join the Liangjiang Aviation swimming competition on the afternoon of the 27th may affect the evening competition, and they cannot join it. The official list of the two teams will be announced tomorrow.

Swimming Training Diagrams (3) Yu Binqi 180

Breaststroke: Mr. Tsuruta, a Japanese athlete who won the 200-meter breaststroke championship at the 10th World Games and set a new record of 2 minutes and 45.4 seconds, has a posture that is completely different from ordinary people. Almost all of his head is exposed above the water. He only lowers his head slightly when moving forward, with the water reaching his mouth. His arms are not completely straightened. When in the cross shape, his palms are bent outwards, and his arms are also turned outwards, which is effective for draining water and moving faster. His leg clamping force is very strong. The diagram is very detailed, and scholars can practice according to the diagram, which will definitely have a considerable effect. In our country's swimming, only Mr. Guo Zhenheng's breaststroke is closest to the world record.

Mr. Leitmeier, a German swimmer, won the 400-meter breaststroke world championship (with a score of 5 minutes and 50.2 seconds).

City Swimming Pool Opens Today 181

The swimming pool of the Municipal Stadium is extremely magnificent and is an open-air style. It is surrounded by bleachers with a seating capacity of 5,000. Under the bleachers are dressing rooms, bathrooms, rest rooms, shops, public toilets, boiler rooms, and water filtration rooms. The pool body is constructed of reinforced concrete and waterproof materials. The bottom and sides of the pool are paved with white mosaics, and the four walls are lined with white ceramic tiles. The entire swimming pool project was completely completed last week. The lowest part of the swimming pool is three feet, and the deepest part is eleven and a half feet. This swimming pool is relatively deep because it is close to the time of the competition. For the convenience of children and those who are not good at swimming, a small swimming pool has been built next to it, with a maximum depth of only two and a half feet. There are also water taps installed next to the pool, which can be used for children to shower. According to reports, the swimming pool will be officially filled with water today.

Education News

Jiangsu Provincial Capital: Implementation Plan for Free Education 183

The Jiangsu Provincial Capital Universal Compulsory Education Committee, convened by the Education Department at 2 PM on the 20th, held a meeting at the Education Department’s auditorium to discuss preparations for compulsory education in the provincial capital. News of this was briefly reported in yesterday's newspaper. The committee members present that day included Lu Xiaobo (Yan Huiyu's representative), Yan Huiyu, Leng Yuqiu, Chuan Zhaoren, Fa Du, Liu Jian, Zhang Zuwu, Feng Ce, Cao Chou, Chen Xifang, Xue Zhongtai (Xue Chuan's representative), Zhao Wuqian (Fa Du's representative), Xie Bin, etc. The meeting was chaired by Chen Xifang. Firstly, the chairman reported on the results of the survey statistics of out-of-school children in the provincial capital and the available school buildings. Secondly, important issues such as the establishment funds for compulsory primary schools in the provincial capital, borrowing school buildings, repairing school buildings, student desks and chairs, teaching equipment, planning purchases, appointing principals, inviting teachers to the province to discuss management methods, and enrolling students were all thoroughly discussed and resolved satisfactorily. The "Jiangsu Provincial Capital 24th Year Free Education Implementation Plan" was also approved. The meeting adjourned at 5 PM.

Jiangsu Provincial Capital 24th Year Free Education Implementation Plan (Passed by the Jiangsu Provincial Capital Universal Compulsory Education Preparatory Committee Meeting in July of the 24th Year) A) General Outline, 1. This plan is based on the Ministry of Education's promulgated "Provisional Measures for the Implementation of Compulsory Education Outline Implementation Rules," the "Jiangsu Province 24th Year Compulsory Education Implementation Plan," and is formulated with reference to the special conditions of the Jiangsu provincial capital urban area. 2. Compulsory education should adhere to the educational objectives of the Republic of China and its implementation guidelines, meet the needs of practical life, and emphasize the cultivation of national consciousness and national concepts. 3. Short-term primary school textbooks and mountain schools are provided free of charge. B) Implementation Steps, 1. Establish the Jiangsu Provincial Capital Universal Compulsory Education Preparatory Committee to coordinate and promote compulsory education in the provincial capital. 2. Investigate out-of-school children and private schools in the province. 3. Raise funds for school buildings and plan equipment. 4. Divide compulsory primary school teaching areas. 5. Name schools according to the names of the townships where each compulsory primary school is located. If there are two or more schools in one township, add sequential distinctions. 6. Select teachers and appoint principals. 7. Promulgate interim regulations and service rules for the appointment, removal, and treatment of principals and teachers in each school. C) Compulsory Enrollment and Delayed/Exempted Enrollment, 1. All school-age children in the provincial capital urban area, except those already enrolled, those who have completed compulsory education, those who have studied in ordinary primary schools for two years, those who have already entered private schools, and those who have been approved for delayed or exempted enrollment, shall be supervised to enter ordinary primary schools or short-term primary schools according to their age and family situation. 2. For those who should enroll but do not, the following procedures shall be followed for parents or guardians: (1) Persuasion; (2) Posting names and issuing warnings; (3) The education department shall, in conjunction with the public security bureau, impose a fine of one to five yuan and still order enrollment within a limited time. 3. In accordance with the regulations of the Ministry of Education, requests for delayed or exempted enrollment that are indeed factual shall be approved accordingly. D) Grade Setting and Organization, 1. Set up 100 grades in the provincial capital urban area. 2. The provincial capital shall set up ordinary primary schools and short-term primary schools according to environmental needs, and set up work-study classes in short-term primary schools as appropriate. 3. Short-term primary schools enroll out-of-school children aged nine to twelve, with a two-part grade system as a principle. Ordinary primary schools should also adopt a two-part zoning half-day two-part system and an intermittent one-part system as much as possible. 4. The number of students per grade is tentatively set at 50 to 70. 5. Utilize private schools, order improvements, and uniformly follow the curriculum of short-term primary schools or ordinary primary schools. Rename them "Improved Private Schools." Those that are well-managed may be directly converted into short-term primary schools or ordinary primary schools. 6. For out-of-school children who cannot attend school due to special difficulties, use mobile teaching methods to remedy this. Their level is the same as that of short-term primary schools. E) School Buildings and Equipment, 1. Short-term primary school buildings should be based on the utilization of existing public offices, ancestral halls, and other houses in the provincial capital, and existing school buildings or social education organizations should be borrowed. 2. When school buildings are insufficient, private houses may be rented or temporary sheds may be built, but efforts must be made to be thrifty and use appropriate construction and leasing funds, which shall be raised by the provincial capital itself. 3. The preparatory expenses for each newly added grade shall be based on local fundraising. F) Curriculum, 1. The curriculum of short-term primary schools shall be handled in accordance with Article 9 of the Ministry of Education's promulgated "Provisional Regulations for One-Year Short-Term Primary Schools." G) Teachers, 1. Teachers and mobile teachers in compulsory primary schools in the provincial capital should be recruited from graduates of provincial and county normal high schools, normal science departments, and rural normal schools. 2. In addition to selecting and recruiting the best graduates from the current provincial normal school, the provincial capital will select and supplement the insufficient number of teachers. 3. Each school has one teacher per grade. H) Funding, 1. The regular expenses for each two-part short-term grade in compulsory primary schools in the provincial capital are tentatively set at 380 yuan per year, and 320 yuan per year for ordinary primary school grades. For 100 grades, approximately 35,000 yuan is needed in total. 2. Grade recurring expenses include the salary and food for two-part short-term primary school teachers, 25 yuan per month, and 22 yuan per month for ordinary primary schools. Maintenance fees are 3 yuan per month each. The remainder is used for purchase costs. Textbooks for short-term primary schools are provided free of charge by the school. 3. The free education funds for the provincial capital are allocated from the Jiangsu Province's 24th Year Promotion of Compulsory Education Funds. 4. The free education funds for the provincial capital are received, distributed, and kept by the Education Department. I) Guidance and Assessment, 1. The Education Department will send personnel to inspect and guide the operation of each primary school in the province and the actual situation of teaching at any time. 2. The performance of each school will be strictly assessed by the inspectors of the Education Department at any time, and rewards and punishments will be determined. 3. Principals and teachers who are deemed by the inspectors to need improvement in their management or teaching methods may be assigned to visit excellent primary schools in the provincial capital at any time to study reform. 4. Teachers and staff of compulsory primary schools in the provincial capital may organize research associations to study important issues such as teaching methods and teaching materials.

Ministry of Education Issues Instruction for Improvement of Jiangsu Provincial Education Institute 188

The Ministry of Education issued an instruction to Jiangsu Provincial Education Institute on the 24th. The original order stated, "The Ministry has sent personnel to inspect the institute. According to the report submitted and reviewed, the teachers of the institute strictly adhere to full-time duties, teaching and guidance, and are generally responsible and conscientious. The students are hardworking and simple, and their discipline is orderly. Many of the various experimental research works are practical. All of these achievements are commendable. However, the following points should be improved immediately: 1. Some of the school buildings of the institute are not strong, and there is a danger of collapse and destruction. Attention should be paid to repair them in order. The scope of the farm is too small and must be expanded to facilitate practice. 2. The experimental area of the institute is limited to one corner, lacking opportunities for comparative research. Efforts should be made to cooperate with administrative agencies, social education agencies, or rural normal schools in other appropriate locations inside and outside the province to promote experimental undertakings. The results of various experimental works currently in progress must be sent to the Ministry from time to time for reference. 3. The equipment of the experimental workshop and various laboratories of the institute is still lacking, and the library also lacks specialized and advanced books. They should be added gradually, weighing the urgent needs. The amount of equipment fees for the institute is too small and should be increased as much as possible in the future to supplement the above-mentioned equipment. 4. The institute's teaching focuses on practical problems, and practice focuses on rural farmland work, which is appropriate. However, the study of agricultural affairs and basic educational knowledge is still insufficient and should be appropriately supplemented. 5. The institute should appropriately increase the number of students recruited from other provinces to broaden training. You are hereby ordered to comply with this and report."

If Church Schools are Not Registered, Student Graduation Qualifications are Invalid - Jiangsu Education Department Explains Doubts 189

The Jiangsu Provincial Education Department, based on the presentation of the Dongtai County Education Association that many church schools do not carry out registration procedures, and questioning the validity of the qualifications of their graduates, made the following special explanation: According to the revised regulations for private schools, private schools that have not completed registration procedures cannot be treated the same as students of private schools that have completed registration procedures. The graduation qualifications of their students cannot be considered valid.

(Guangzhou Correspondence) The Guangdong Provincial Government has decided to add four provincial secondary schools in the 24th year: one is the Provincial Changsha Normal School, one is the Provincial Laolong Normal School, one is the Provincial Sports College, and one is the Provincial Fisheries Vocational School. Huang Linshu, Director of the Education Department, has accompanied technician He Juncheng to inspect the site of Changsha Normal School, and sent inspector Huang Guojun and commissioner Cheng Yiyue to Shantou to inspect the site of the Fisheries School. Beiyang Institute of Technology: Mining and Metallurgy Department Ready 191

(Tianjin, 24th) The mining and metallurgy department of the Beiyang Institute of Technology Engineering Research Institute is fully prepared. The department is divided into three branches: mining engineering, metallurgical engineering, and applied geology. Graduate students can choose one branch to study, with the other two as auxiliary. The term is tentatively set at four semesters. In the first two semesters, 12 to 15 credits are required, and in the third and fourth semesters, 9 to 12 credits are required. In addition to the existing equipment, the department is using huge sums of money to purchase new equipment from overseas.

Report on the Closing of the Annual Meeting of the China Vocational Education Society: All Proposals Reviewed and Approved; Location of Next Meeting Decided 192

(Qingdao Correspondence) The 15th Annual Meeting of the China Vocational Education Society and the 13th National Vocational Education Discussion Conference opened at the Municipal Girls' Middle School in this city. Group meetings were held in succession to review various proposals, which have generally come to a satisfactory conclusion. The second general meeting was held this morning (21st), and the closing ceremony was held in the afternoon. The details are recorded as follows:

Second General Meeting

At 8:00 AM on this day, the second general meeting was still held in the auditorium of the Municipal Girls' Middle School. Chairman Ou Yuanhuai, after opening the meeting as usual, asked the directors of each group to report on the results of the review: (1) Wei Mingchu reported on the results of the review of the vocational school curriculum group; (2) Zhang Boyin reported on the results of the review of the vocational guidance and supplementary education group; (3) Guo Baolin reported on the results of the review of the rural improvement group; (4) Zhang Jundu reported on the results of the review of the home economics education group; (5) Ou Yuanhuai reported on the results of the review of the administrative group. After each group reported, the discussion began. 1. All cases of the administrative group were voted on according to the results of the review and passed. 2. All cases of the vocational school curriculum group were voted on according to the results of the review and passed. 3. All cases of the vocational guidance and supplementary education group, except for the 25th case which was revised and supplemented, were voted on according to the results of the review and passed. 4. All cases of the rural improvement group were voted on according to the results of the review and passed. 5. All cases of the home economics education group were voted on according to the revised methods and passed.

Temporary Proposals

(1) Please set up a vocational guidance center in Qingdao as a memorial to this conference of the Society. Reasons: Qingdao has convenient transportation and developed industry and commerce, and is a famous commercial port in the country. In recent years, education has become even more developed. The municipal authorities pay great attention to the issues of further education and employment for young people, and there are already vocational guidance committees and vocational guidance departments in various schools. Recently, personnel matters have become increasingly complex, and employers feel the lack of talent, and job seekers suffer from the lack of employment opportunities. The mismatch between supply and demand is such that the prosperity of the city and the improvement of the profession depend on a guidance agency to plan and strategize. It is appropriate to set up a special agency to preside over its affairs, so as to achieve perfection. This Society is holding an annual meeting in Qingdao this time, hoping to make a contribution and exert a slight effect. It is proposed that the Qingdao Municipal Government set up a vocational guidance center as a memorial to this conference of the Society. Is this appropriate? Please vote on it. Method: This Society will send a letter to the Qingdao Municipal Administrative Authorities to designate a preparatory committee to start preparations and complete them as soon as possible. Proposers: Liu Zhanen and Pan Wenan from the Shanghai Vocational Guidance Center. (2) Please hold the next conference in Xi'an. Proposal by Shui Jimei, representative of the Gansu Education Department. (3) Please hold the 16th conference in Guangxi as decided by the previous conference. Proposal by Society member Yang Weiyu and others. The above two cases were discussed together, and it was decided that the location would be Xi'an, Nanning, or other places, and the time would be summer or winter vacation, which would be selected by the Society at that time.

Implementation Guidelines

At the end of each conference, there is a declaration to be issued to the society, or a telegram to be submitted to the government. This conference decided to change the method, and simply formulated five articles based on the goals commonly recognized by colleagues, as guidelines for implementation and promotion: (1) Vocational school education, vocational supplementary education, and vocational guidance advocate that the three should be given equal importance at the same time, and vocational supplementary education should be given special attention in light of the current needs of China. (2) Vocational schools that have been established must strengthen their content and practically plan the graduates' future. Vocational schools that are planned to be established should carefully examine social needs and proceed cautiously. (3) Agricultural education advocates that it should be implemented practically under the entire rural improvement plan. In addition to vocational schools that must be handled in accordance with the previous article and rural primary schools that must focus on production education, it is advocated that short-term training classes and lectures should be held frequently, anytime, anywhere, and for anything to popularize agricultural education and train agricultural technology. 4. Women's home economics must pay special attention to research and promotion. (5) Cultivating national patriotic sentiments and enhancing young people's service morality and intelligence must be given special attention when implementing vocational education. It is hoped that this positive spirit of civic training will permeate all vocational education institutions. It is recognized that young people being educated cannot complete the mission of vocational education without this spirit.

Closing Ceremony

At the closing ceremony of the conference, Chairman Lei Fazhang, Jiang Hengyuan, Huang Renzhi, Shen Xinqing, and Ou Yuanhuai performed the ceremony as usual. First, Jiang Hengyuan gave a speech, which was roughly divided into five points: (1) The recent floods are serious and we should commemorate the compatriots who were killed to express our condolences. (All stood up and remained silent for three minutes.) (2) Thank you for the enthusiastic support of all sectors of Qingdao. A formal thank you is extended in the name of the conference. (3) I apologize for the inadequate reception due to the small number of people in the office of the Vocational Education Society coming to Qingdao. Please forgive me. (4) I am very sorry that I was unable to have in-depth talks with the members who attended the meeting due to the short time in the past few days. I plan to wait for instructions in the members' lounge from 2:30 PM to 3:30 PM today. (5) The proposals of the conference were hastily discussed and may not be entirely appropriate. If any inappropriate places are discovered afterwards, please send a letter to give instructions so as to increase effectiveness. Then Lei Fazhang gave a speech, roughly divided into three points: (1) I apologize for the inadequate preparation and reception beforehand. (2) The spirit of unity of the Vocational Education Society has a great influence on all undertakings. Promoting and carrying forward this spirit can revive the nation. (3) I hope that everyone can take the national crisis as a prerequisite and shoulder the responsibility of saving the country and seeking to be in charge. Shen Xinqing then gave a speech, which roughly said that the three days of the conference had passed in a hurry, and there were many feelings. Whether the excellent reception of the Qingdao Municipal Government and all sectors of society and what this conference has contributed to the local area are commensurate, I ask myself that there are still many shameful things. I hope that after you members return, you will all shoulder the heavy responsibility of saving the country and develop from your own position under the grand goal of reviving the nation, and contribute to the society. At the same time, help the vocational education cause and spread the light. This is to answer the grand speech of the reception of all sectors of this city. After the speech was finished, the conference concluded successfully.

Commercial News

Finance Overseas Emptying Theories; Gold Price Shows Slight Decline 196

Midday market conditions extremely calm; Result: a rollback of three yuan and five jiao

Yesterday's gold market saw overseas silver market failing to align, major bulls already selling off, wavering sentiment, coupled with unfavorable overseas news, leading to a decline. However, it rebounded easily after hitting lows. The morning session was extremely quiet with limited fluctuations. Initially, the overseas silver market showed no changes; Monte Carlo forward silver rose by 1.5 to 2 li. Exchange rate fluctuations were minimal. London spot gold contracted by three and a half pence. Off-exchange preliminary trading opened, immediately dropping to 55.60 yuan. Reuters reported that US Senator Pittman stated that the Treasury Department was still proceeding with silver purchases, believing that a price of $1.29 per ounce was inevitable. It was said that the Monte Carlo futures silver market was affected by his remarks and rose, which was taken as news to sell. It soon retreated to 52.30 yuan, before major players stepped in to cover, stabilizing the market. The Central Bank's official exchange rates showed no changes for both British and American currencies. Customs gold units contracted by three li. The standard price for gold was reduced to 865.70 yuan, without much impact. After the opening, banks showed strong appetite, traders followed suit, pushing prices upward. The Central Bank releasing spot shillings caused a slight decline. The HSBC's exchange rate listing remained unchanged, and sentiment stabilized. Later, with HSBC's efforts to buy in, prices rose temporarily. Banks took the opportunity to release, and sellers began to become active, gradually driving prices lower. However, fluctuations were frequent along the way, ultimately with limited transactions. The foreign exchange market stabilized, and market conditions were extremely quiet. The afternoon session was mediocre for a long time. Although the Central Bank continued to release, and the Indian silver forecast of Zhang San'an was made, market sentiment was extremely calm. Banks were also actively trading with each other. Even if there was a small setback, it quickly stabilized. The market closed slightly higher. The midday session saw initial fatigue followed by stability, with a slight settling of trends. The midday market conditions are recorded as follows.

The morning opened at 853.20 yuan, a setback of 6.20 yuan compared to the previous close, then 2.80 yuan. Overseas Chinese HSBC were both buying US dollars for September at 18.75. Dada, Hengyu, Huixiang, Qingfa, Yongyuanchang, Yongyongli, Yuanmao Yong, etc. were all buying. Fuxing Yong, Dada Decheng came out and then re-entered, gradually rising to 6.30 yuan. Fuxing Yong, Chunyuan Yong, Hengyu took advantage of the high prices to supply contracts, falling to 4.70 yuan. Pre-knowing HSBC's exchange rate listing, British and American were both flat and still rising, Hengyu, Chunyuan Yong, Yuanmao Yong came in, again rising to 5.90 yuan. At this time, the Central Bank released spot shillings, Fuxing Yongli sold and continued to rise, HSBC vigorously bought spot shillings at 8.75, Mitsui ate August at 68.75, Huixiang, Richang, Yuanchang, Hengyu, Dada Decheng all bought, then rose to 7.10 yuan. Chunyuan, Hengyu took advantage of the high price to sell, retreating to 5.20 yuan. Fuxing Yong, Shunmao still deposited, rising to 6.70 yuan. HSBC came to sell August US dollars at half a yuan, Hongkang, Yongwanxing, Tongyi, Pachangyong sold in succession, falling to 4.60 yuan, Lichang, Tongyu Run, retail investors Qianchang, Xiangfu Taiyong, Xiangfeng, etc. collectively entered slightly, gradually rising to 6.30 yuan. The Central Bank came out with spot shillings at 8.75, Chunyuan Yong, Yuanmao Yong, Fuxing Yongchang, Dayingxiang sold and repaired, falling to 4.30 yuan. Yu Fuxing Yong, Yuqing Yong, Yuanyishen Feng jointly deposited contracts, again rising to 6 yuan, predicting Indian silver Dayi Er'anna, Hengchang Yong, Huixiang sold contracts, falling to 4.70 yuan. Fuxing Yong, Yuanmao Yong still bought, noon closed again rose to 855.90 yuan, after the close Hengyu, Fuxing Yong, Shunmao, etc. all bought, rising to over 7 yuan, check the highest price in the afternoon 857.10 yuan, the lowest price 852.80 yuan, a total of 4.30 yuan fluctuations, the result compared to the previous close fell 3.50 yuan.

Oil Market: Asphalt Autumn Sales Approaching 208

Asphalt typically sees little market activity during the summer off-season. However, as the autumn paving season approaches, local merchants are preparing to supply the market. Due to limited stock, they are closely monitoring incoming shipments. However, transportation is difficult during the hot weather, delaying action. Although the Hankou market appears weak, prices could easily rise once trading begins, as inventory is low and merchants are unwilling to sell at low prices. Maché asphalt once sold for eleven taels and four qian but now requires eleven taels and six qian. Heavy Jing asphalt still demands twelve taels per unit, demonstrating market resilience. Zhejiang asphalt market news is subdued, likely because little attention is paid to off-season goods. However, the trees in Jiahe, western Zhejiang, are bearing fruit. Current observations suggest a successful harvest, barring unforeseen events. New crop yields are expected to be several times higher than last winter. However, it is hard to predict whether sales will increase. Over-supply when the new crop arrives could dramatically alter the market.
